Current Commentary

The International Difficulties of the German-Austrian Merger 24

The recent Austrian incident has caused anxiety among countries such as France and Italy, fearing it might lead to a disguised merger between Germany and Austria, disrupting the balance of power in Europe. We already mentioned this yesterday. However, a German-Austrian merger faces numerous difficulties and is impossible without forcibly tearing up the post-World War I treaties.

Some argue that for the resurgence of Germany's national fortunes, the most urgent priority is to unite all Germanic peoples. Among Germanic peoples outside Germany, the most numerous reside in present-day Austria. Therefore, a German-Austrian merger is a necessary tactic to promote Pan-Germanism. If it becomes a reality, most of the shackles imposed on Germany by the Treaty of Versailles can be removed, and Germany's land and population will be restored to pre-war levels. Then, the eastward movement initiated before the war might have a chance of success.

Such are the aspirations of the Germans. If they could achieve their wishes, they would inevitably reshape the map of Europe today, triggering a second world war. Its peaceful success is unlikely. France, Germany's historical enemy, will certainly do its utmost to hinder Germany's resurgence to avoid any hidden dangers in the east. Secondly, Italy opposes the German-Austrian merger. If the merger is achieved, the buffer zone between Germany and Italy will be completely removed, subsequently endangering Italy's hegemony in the Adriatic Sea and the development of the Balkan Peninsula, the consequences of which are unpredictable. Moreover, after the war, Italy seized Austria's southern territories, incorporating 250,000 local Germans. If Germany and Austria merge, the flames of Pan-Germanism will become irresistible. These 250,000 Germans will inevitably rise up to seek liberation from foreign subjugation and allegiance to Germany. This issue of ethnic minorities is also a major concern for the Italians and cannot be ignored. Thirdly, there is Czechoslovakia. Czechoslovakia is located north of present-day Austria, and its western part penetrates into German territory. If Germany and Austria merge, Czechoslovakia would be surrounded by Germany on three sides. In addition, Czechoslovakia currently has 3.2 million Germans, and its fear of Pan-Germanism far exceeds that of Italy. As for Poland, although it has a ten-year non-aggression pact with Germany, it has over 2 million Germans within its borders. Therefore, it should also have similar concerns about the German-Austrian merger. Among European countries, only Britain, which does not have significant conflicts of interest with Germany, is more sympathetic to Germany. However, Britain is also a signatory to the Treaty of Versailles and is unlikely to ignore France's request to jointly uphold the treaty. Furthermore, since Hitler came to power, his various actions have been violent and arbitrary, greatly undermining British goodwill. Therefore, its attitude towards the Austrian incident is also consistent with that of France and Italy.

Given so many international difficulties, Hitler of Germany has only two paths to take. One is unconditional surrender, and the other is to overcome all difficulties and seize power in Austria. According to recent foreign news, the German Social Party has already demanded that the Austrian Prime Minister resign automatically. It is clear which path they are taking. What we can foresee here is that Austrian chaos may recur. At that time, France, Italy, and other countries will also take effective measures to fulfill their long-standing desire to maintain Austria's independence. If so, the clouds of war will reappear in Europe. We shall wait and see.

Our Government Issues Order to Mourn the Death of the King of Belgium 25

National Government Offices Fly Flags at Half-Mast for Three Days

European Royals All Participate in Funeral

(Nanjing) The Executive Yuan, considering the close relations between China and Belgium and the passing of the King of Belgium, in addition to Chairman Lin's telegraphic condolences, the Executive Yuan meeting on the 20th resolved to present to the National Government an order to all government agencies nationwide to fly flags at half-mast for three days starting from the 20th to express condolences. It is reported that the King of Belgium's funeral will be held on the 22nd, and the Crown Prince will ascend the throne on the 23rd. (Central News Agency, 20th)

(Nanjing) All government agencies in the capital city have flown flags at half-mast for three days starting from the 20th to mourn the King of Belgium. Furthermore, all foreign embassies in Beijing have also flown flags at half-mast for the King of Belgium starting from the 20th. (Special Dispatch, 20th)

Ten Thousand Mourners at the Palace Gates 26

Still Streaming Through Late at Night

Brussels: The funeral of the late King of Belgium is scheduled to be held in this church on Thursday. The coffin will be placed in the church and then moved to the Laeken Royal Palace for burial. The new king is scheduled to be sworn in on Friday. Before the inauguration, administrative affairs will be temporarily managed by the cabinet. Up to ten thousand people have signed the condolence book at the palace, and the stream continues late into the night. (Guomin News Agency, 19th)

Brussels: When the remains of the King of Belgium were moved from the Laeken Royal Palace in the suburbs to the Royal Palace in the capital yesterday, more than one hundred thousand Belgians stood silently by the roadside, expressing their deep sorrow. The King's coffin was covered with the Belgian flag and carried on a gun carriage, with six people carrying torches leading the way. The Belgian Crown Prince and his brother, Prince Charles, followed the carriage in military uniforms, followed by veterans and representatives of various organizations. The Crown Prince is scheduled to be sworn in on Friday and has now been promoted to the rank of Lieutenant General. The Belgian Royal Family has announced a six-month mourning period. At the King's burial, four Crown Princes of European kingdoms will represent their fathers in attending the funeral, namely the Crown Prince of Italy, the Crown Prince of Britain, the Crown Prince of Norway, and the Crown Prince of Sweden. The King of Bulgaria and the King of Siam, who are currently touring Europe, will both personally attend the funeral. The Queen of the Netherlands will be represented by her husband, the King of Romania by his brother, Prince Nicholas, and the King of Denmark by his son.

Since the death of the King of Belgium, members of the Royal Family have been visiting the Queen. The British Emperor has dispatched Admiral Keyes, commander of the British fleet, to accompany the British Crown Prince to Belgium. If the weather is good, the British Crown Prince and Keyes will travel by plane. When the House of Commons met yesterday afternoon, the Speaker and others were in mourning. After the question time in the House of Commons, Prime Minister MacDonald made a speech, stating that the British people were deeply saddened by the news of the death of the King of Belgium and believed that the members of Parliament would wish to express their condolences to the Belgian Royal Family and people. The Prime Minister then announced that he would propose a motion tomorrow calling on the British Emperor to send a telegram to the new King of Belgium expressing the House of Commons' deep condolences to the Belgian Royal Family and people. The House of Commons usually makes such a proposal when the head of a friendly country passes away, and the House of Lords will follow suit. (Reuters, 20th)

Brussels: French Prime Minister Doumergue, accompanied by his staff, visited the Queen of Belgium in Brussels to offer condolences and laid a wreath at the late King's shrine. He has now returned to Paris. (Guomin News Agency, 20th)

Rome: The Italian Crown Prince, Prince Umberto, son-in-law of King Albert of Belgium, departed last night at midnight for Brussels to participate in Albert's funeral. (Havas News Agency, 20th)

Sofia: King Boris of Bulgaria, accompanied by Prince Cyril and his entourage, departed last night for Brussels to participate in the King of Belgium's funeral. (Havas News Agency, 20th)

(Beiping) After the death of King Albert I of Belgium, the embassies of various countries in Beiping have lowered their flags to half-mast to express condolences, with the Belgian and Dutch embassies lowering their flags for two weeks, the British, American, German, and French embassies for one week, and the Japanese embassy for three days. Various government agencies in Beiping have also been ordered to lower their flags to half-mast for three days. (Special Dispatch, 20th)

No Concrete Decision Yet on Italian Boxer Indemnity Treasury Bonds 27

(Nanjing) Kong Xiangxi returned to Beijing in the same car with Zhang Xueliang this morning. According to those around Kong, in order to make up for the lack of finances and hoping to tide over the difficulties, Kong had discussed with the Shanghai banking community borrowing a new loan of 44 million yuan with the Italian Boxer Indemnity as collateral. Then, issuing new treasury bonds of over 40 million yuan with the Italian Boxer Indemnity as collateral is a misunderstanding of the rumors. The so-called new treasury bonds were proposed by the Shanghai banking community, as the collateral fund for the new loan borrowed by the Ministry is solid, the banking community then transferred this Italian Boxer Indemnity collateral as collateral to issue new treasury bonds, and it was not a motion from the Ministry. Currently, all methods are still under discussion and there is no concrete decision yet. (Special Dispatch, 20th)

New Court Organization Law 28

Will Be Implemented in the Next Fiscal Year

(Nanjing) An official from the Ministry of Justice said that the Ministry plans to implement the new Court Organization Law in the second half of the 23rd fiscal year. However, there are quite a few county courts in the current three-level four-instance system for the first instance. In the future, after implementation, if these county courts are changed to branch courts of the district courts, they will handle first-instance cases at the same time as the district courts. Also, after the implementation of the three-level three-instance system, the number of cases in the high courts and the Supreme Court will increase sharply. In the future, in order to meet the needs of reality, the high courts in various provinces will inevitably add some branch courts, and the Supreme Court will also increase the number of divisions to handle the cases. (Special Dispatch, 20th)

Pingjin Match Industry Agrees on Relief Measures 29

(Tianjin) On the 19th, the Pingjin Match Industry responded to Ning Encheng's call and met in Beijing to discuss relief measures, deciding on four items: 1. The preferential measures that the government gives to other regions should be applied equally to this region. 2. The impact on businesses and factories in this region due to strict compliance with laws and regulations should be relieved by the government at the same time. 3. The match sticks from other regions that have not been reported by the factory representatives stationed in that region should be inspected piece by piece by the inspection offices in this region and affixed with inspection labels to prove it. 4. Businesses and factories intend to organize a public sales agency, and the local bureau will assist in promoting it. The above measures will be implemented after submission to and approval by the Ministry of Finance. (Special Dispatch, 20th)

Shandong Provincial Government Plans to Establish Pawnshops in Various Counties 30

(Jinan) At today's regular meeting of the provincial government, it was resolved to: 1. Form the Budget Review Committee for the 23rd fiscal year. 2. Plan to establish pawnshops in various counties, with 20% of the shares held by the government and 80% by businesses. Initially, one pawnshop will be established in each of Weixian, Liaocheng, Jining, and Fushan, each with a capital of 50,000 yuan. The remaining counties may jointly establish a pawnshop, with capital divided into four levels: 10,000, 20,000, 30,000, and 40,000. The Finance and Construction Departments will summon the chairmen of the chambers of commerce of various counties to the provincial capital to discuss the implementation. (Special Dispatch, 20th)

Italian-German Rivalry for Austria Causes a Direct Conflict 47

Italy Warns Germany Not to Interfere in Austrian Affairs

Germany Declares a Ten-Day Truce with Austria

Austria Expresses Distrust Towards Germany

Rome: The Italian newspaper "Il Popolo d'Italia," the official newspaper of Italian Prime Minister Mussolini, published an article today warning Germany not to interfere in Austrian affairs. The wording was unusually stern, stating that the joint declaration of Britain, France, and Italy affirmed the necessity of maintaining Austria's integrity and independence and had laid out a path for a united attitude and, when necessary, united action. There is now no doubt that the recent violent actions of the National Socialist Party in Austria were instigated by the Germans. Most of the murder weapons in Austria came from Germany. Italy wants a fair revision of the treaties, but this cannot be interpreted as allowing people to do whatever they want. It only wants to seek a collective and regulated restoration of countries and territories based on recognized justice. Italy will never give up its responsibilities and obligations as a major power. The views expressed in Italian newspapers must be strictly checked, so the above remarks are noteworthy. (Reuters, 19th)

Munich: Today, National Socialist Party propagandist Habicht presented Prime Minister Dollfuss and the Austrian government with a truce. Habicht, speaking to all of Austria through a powerful radio broadcast, stated that the National Socialist Party is now giving Prime Minister Dollfuss a ten-day truce period to consider his resignation and the demand for closer cooperation with Germany. The truce period expires on the 28th. During this truce period, all National Socialist Party members are prohibited from attacking the government with force or propaganda. If the Austrian government does not accept this demand or its response is not satisfactory, "then war will begin again after the truce period expires." Habicht has repeatedly advised the military and civilians to join the organization he leads to drive out Prime Minister Dollfuss and form a new government with the National Socialist Party. According to observers, Austria's "Little Napoleon" has three paths to take: (1) Use force to curb the attacks of the National Socialist Party; (2) Accept the demands of the National Socialist Party and retire; (3) Appeal to the League of Nations. Observers continued that the German Social Party could obliterate the recent tripartite declaration signed by Britain, France, and Italy with cunning words. The National Socialist Party claimed that the German government did not want to force out Prime Minister Dollfuss. It was the National Socialist Party that wanted to drive Prime Minister Dollfuss out of Vienna and seize power. Prime Minister Dollfuss was extremely opposed to submitting this dispute to the League of Nations. Now Dollfuss may not be able to avoid taking this approach. Most of Austria has held demonstrations, and there have been clashes between the National Socialist Party and the police. (Guomin News Agency, 19th)

Vienna: German National Socialist Party propagandist Habicht gave a speech in Munich yesterday, saying that the truce between Germany and Austria would last until February 26. The Vienna newspapers did not know about this news at all. Reporters and officials generally believe that Habicht's attitude is a common tactic and is actually unfounded. The Austrian government stated that Vienna has not received any proposals from the German government, and that while Germany is proposing peace, it is also asking Austrian Social Party members to join the National Socialist Party, which shows no sincerity. Therefore, all parties do not pay attention to Habicht's speech. (Havas News Agency, 20th)

Joint Declaration of England, France, and Italy 48

Austria Welcomes It But Remains Pessimistic

German Newspaper Makes a Jesting Comment

(Vienna) The governments of England, France, and Italy have issued a joint declaration asserting the maintenance of Austrian independence. Austrian government officials consider this proof of aid to Austria and express their great welcome. However, they are quite pessimistic about whether this declaration will have any real effect. They believe that the issue of German-Austrian relations should still be submitted to the League of Nations for handling, and that this should be done very soon. (20th Havas dispatch)

(Berlin) Today, a semi-official diplomatic and political commentary newspaper in Berlin published an article stating that the reason France initiated the joint declaration by England, France, and Italy to maintain Austrian independence was that the French government was deeply weary of the issue of military disarmament. Therefore, it fabricated this matter in order to slightly divert the attention of world opinion. There is a kind of agreement being formed between England, Italy, and Germany. The declaration by England, Germany, and Italy on the Austrian matter is no less than a countermeasure to this agreement. The newspaper further stated that although the French government has repeatedly stated that the three-nation declaration was initiated by Paris, Italy had actually had this intention for some time. The reason England and Italy jointly issued the declaration with France was simply that they did not want to trouble the League of Nations with this matter, or take other more inappropriate international steps, so they merely played along with France. Therefore, judging from the established facts, this three-nation declaration cannot be regarded as a victory for French policy, but rather as a failure of Austrian actions. Austria wanted to have this matter handled by the League of Nations, or thereby internationalize the internal turmoil. All such attempts have utterly failed. The Dolfuss government of Austria harbors prejudice and willingly allows the situation to worsen. Fortunately, its request has been rejected, giving Germany a complete victory. As for the maintenance of Austrian independence and territorial integrity mentioned in the three-nation declaration, and that existing treaties should not be violated, these are perfectly in line with German Chancellor Hitler's declaration not to interfere in Austria's internal affairs by force and not to violate any treaties related to Austria. (19th National dispatch)

(Berlin) Newspapers here comment on the joint declaration issued by England, France, and Italy, advocating the maintenance of Austrian independence, expressing extreme dissatisfaction with Italy. The semi-official diplomatic correspondence newspaper advocates that Germany adopt a new strategy to deal with the situation, namely, if the Austrian issue is to be discussed by the League of Nations or internationally as advocated by various countries, then Germany should demand that the issue of German-Austrian unification be decided by a referendum of Austrian citizens. (20th Havas dispatch)

Anglo-Russian Trade Agreement Announced 57

Smooth Turn in Relations Between the Two Countries

British Goods Exports to Russia Expected to Increase Greatly

(London) The newly established Anglo-Russian trade agreement was announced today. Its content is indeed as expected, with the main purpose of balancing the amount of trade between the two countries. It stipulates that the ratio of goods exported from Russia to goods exported from Britain to Russia will be 1.7 to 1.0 in 1934, and will be reduced to 1.1 to 1.0 by 1938. British exports to Russia are expected to increase greatly in the future, because the ratio last year was one to four. In the agreement, the Soviet Union agrees to have commercial disputes handled by English courts. Both parties may terminate this agreement by giving six months' notice, and it is stipulated that Soviet goods will receive most-favored-nation treatment in all parts of the British Empire, with the exception of the Dominions. (19th Reuters dispatch)

(London) The trade agreement signed between the United Kingdom and the Soviet Union is a temporary agreement, and its terms have just been announced. There are two very novel points. The first point comes from the Ottawa Agreement, which guarantees the preferential tariff treatment obtained by the British Dominions so as not to be affected by the excessively low prices of Soviet goods. Those whose economies are controlled by the state can cause prices to plummet or maintain goods that were originally low in price without rising. The second point is that the United Kingdom and the Soviet Union should restore the balance of trade with each other. The agreement stipulates on the first point, "If the value of goods exported by one contracting country affects the preferential treatment and causes inconvenience to the local products of the other contracting country, then the other country may notify the first country of this matter." It is also stipulated that in such cases, both parties will negotiate. If the negotiations fail, the affected country may declare that it will suspend the application of most-favored-nation treatment to the relevant goods three months after the date of the first notification. In addition to stipulating the minimum price of goods exported by both parties, the agreement limits the ratio of the amount of trade between the two countries in order to seek a balance in business between them. According to this ratio, the first year's Soviet exports are compared to British exports, with a ratio of one to seven, which will gradually decrease to one to one. In addition, the United Kingdom continues to grant diplomatic personnel privileges to the Soviet trade delegation. The agreement has no fixed term of validity, but either party may declare it abolished by giving three months' prior notice. (19th Havas)

(Moscow) The Pravda newspaper commented on the signing of the trade agreement with the Soviet Union, saying, "This agreement will lay the foundation for an important development in normal economic relations between the United Kingdom and the Soviet Union, and at the same time, it will be a turning point, so that relations between the proletarian country and one of the world's largest capitalist countries will gradually improve, and a new factor will be added to the promotion of peace. The signing of this agreement was the result of long and protracted negotiations (for which the Soviet Union bears no responsibility). At the same time, the agreement will undoubtedly be a head-on blow to the plans of those who are obsessed with the anti-Soviet economic war, such as Conservative Party adventurers and a large number of politicians suffering from hysteria. As for those who intend to use provocative and military adventurous policies to destroy commercial relations with the Soviet Union, they should also receive a warning. The Soviet Union's public opinion naturally welcomes the fact that the more far-sighted and sound views of a part of the British bourgeoisie have been able to overcome their views with a tendency towards adventure. "(18th Tass dispatch)

Poland Does Not Abandon the Gold Standard 58

(Warsaw) Polish Minister of Finance Zawadzki told guests today that Poland intends to maintain the gold standard and will not follow the Czech Republic in reducing the value of its currency. Poland currently has a trade surplus, domestic prices are low, and the amount of domestic debt it owes is not much. There is absolutely no worry in the next few years. Therefore, Poland will not abandon the gold standard under any circumstances. (19th National Society dispatch)

Cotton Industry Negotiations: British and Japanese Views Clash 59

Lancashire Pays Attention to Today's Meeting

(London) Talks between the British and Japanese cotton industries will resume tomorrow. The attention of people in Lancashire is focused on this. After the talks last week, the British representatives sent a document to the Japanese representatives, clearly stating that Lancashire's position is that any agreement must cover the world market. This position directly contradicts the Japanese side's first step, which is to require that the scope of application of the agreement be limited to British colonies. This restriction is not acceptable to Lancashire, as the discussion only covers one-tenth of Lancashire's export market. It will be known tomorrow what concessions the Japanese side is prepared to make. However, judging from recent phenomena, the Japanese representatives do not seem prepared to make much concessions. A detailed examination of the cotton import figures for British colonies reveals the extent of the Japanese cotton goods' intrusion. Western Africa is Lancashire's most important export market. Last year, Lancashire's exports decreased from 159 million yards to 102 million yards. The most-favored-nation treatment clause was revoked a few months ago as a method to prevent the intrusion of Japanese goods. British cloth imports in Ceylon were 32.1 million yards in 1927, but had decreased to 15.8 million yards by 1932, while Japanese cotton cloth increased from 6.1 million yards to 40.4 million yards. Japan's exports to Sudan increased from 35 million yards in 1929 to 42 million yards in 1932, while Lancashire's exports fell from 11.1 million yards to 6.6 million yards. Japan's cotton trade in Kenya and Uganda in Africa increased from 14.6 million yards to 30 million yards between 1928 and 1932, while Lancashire's decreased from 9.5 million yards to 5.7 million yards. At the same time, the quantity of Japanese cotton cloth imported into Tanganyika in Africa increased from 9.2 million yards to 21.9 million yards, while the quantity of goods imported by Lancashire decreased by half, to 4.6 million yards. Last year, Lancashire's exports to Hong Kong also decreased greatly, from 52,866,800 yards to 18,618,300 yards. (20th Reuters dispatch)

Next Year's Naval Conference 64

Naval Vessel Tonnage to Be Significantly Modified

(Geneva) According to naval experts here, the 1935 Naval Conference will significantly modify naval vessel tonnage limits, intending to reduce the maximum tonnage from 35,000 tons to 30,000 or 25,000 tons. Although the United States is making every effort to oppose the reduction of naval vessel tonnage, there are currently no plans to build large warships, and the government's attitude has recently changed. Previously, the United Kingdom, Japan, France, and Italy all discussed reducing naval vessel tonnage in Geneva, with only the United States strongly opposing it. The United Kingdom intends to change the maximum tonnage to 22,000 tons, while Japan intends to change it to 25,000 tons. Smaller naval powers all intend to change the maximum limit to 10,000 tons. However, detailed investigations reveal that no country has built extremely large tonnage vessels after the war. The United Kingdom has fifteen large warships, with the Hood being the largest, at 42,100 tons, launched in 1920. The remaining ships are around 29,150 tons. The total tonnage of British warships is 474,750 tons. The United States also has fifteen large warships, with the Pennsylvania being the largest, at 33,100 tons. The smallest, the Arkansas, is 26,100 tons. The total tonnage of the U.S. Navy's warships is 455,450 tons. In the past, the United States strongly advocated building large tonnage warships for the sake of fully protecting its territories, but according to experts' research, 25,000-ton vessels are also quite applicable. Japan has ten large warships, with a total tonnage of 298,400 tons. Japan is concerned about the powerful U.S. Navy, so it strongly advocates reducing naval vessel tonnage. (20th National News Agency Telegram)

(Washington) The Vinson Naval Bill, previously passed in the House of Representatives, is being formally discussed in the Senate today. According to the proposal, it aims to build 120 warships and 1,184 naval aircraft to the maximum extent possible under the Naval Conference Treaty. Given the current global situation, destroyers, submarines, and aircraft are the most important. The United States is currently building an aircraft carrier weighing 15,000 tons, which will soon be completed. (19th National News Agency Telegram)

Soviet Russia Expands Air Force 65

Borrowing $2.5 Million from the U.S.

Ordering Aircraft and Opening Factories in Russia

(Washington) Today, Eugene Chen, General Manager of the Curtiss-Wright Airplane Company, stated that the Soviet Russian government is currently in negotiations with the U.S. government to order aircraft engine contracts, requiring a loan of approximately $2.5 million. He also said that the company had manufactured aircraft engines for Soviet Russia and will now fully deliver them. The current plan is to establish a factory in Russia and send American technicians to provide guidance. It is said that the Soviet Russian authorities intend to build the Soviet Russian army into the world's number one, as countries are currently competing on naval issues. According to military experts' observations, the Russian air force already ranks second in the world, superior to the British and American, only slightly inferior to the French. It is said that Russia can produce 35 aircraft per day. Once problems arise in the Far East, or in a war with Japan, it will be well-equipped to cope. As for the Soviet Russian government's negotiations with the U.S. government to borrow money, with the recent cooperation between the U.S. and Russia, this matter will likely succeed. (19th National News Agency Telegram)

Upholding Freedom of Speech

Five-Day Work Week

(Washington) President Roosevelt today approved the newspaper industry code, which has been drafted for several months. President Roosevelt requested that newspapers in major cities with circulations of over 75,000 copies should immediately base their employees' working hours on a five-day work week totaling forty hours. (19th Reuters Telegram)

(Washington) President Roosevelt recently signed the newspaper regulations, the content of which only deals with unfair business competition. The issues of working hours and wages will be resolved two months later. According to the new regulations, children under the age of sixteen will not be allowed to sell newspapers on the streets at night. The regulations also contain a declaration upholding the principle of freedom of speech, but newspapers have no right to violate news that is obscene or defamatory, as prohibited by law. (19th Havas Telegram)

National Resistance West of the Ussuri River (Harbin Correspondence) 86

The Blood and Tears of the Northeastern People

Japan's Controlled Economy

The Hardships and Destitution of the Peasants

The three northeastern provinces have been ravaged by the Japanese army for more than two years. Now, there is hardly any place without Japanese troops. The three northeastern provinces are almost entirely under Japanese rule, but there is one exception: the northeastern part of Jilin, the triangle along the Ussuri River to the intersection of the Heilongjiang River, namely the three counties of Fuyuan, Raohe, and Hulin, still proudly displaying the Blue Sky White Sun flag and continuing to maintain the Republic of China's era name. Someone came from Raohe the day before yesterday. According to what he said, the most difficult thing there is the sparse population, the difficulty of providing supplies, and the lack of bullets, which are relatively minor matters. Because the Righteous Army there was not formed by outlaws or regular troops at the beginning, but by local Red Spear Society and Big Sword Society members. A year and a half ago, they were only armed with nationalistic zeal, holding knives and guns and fighting desperately with the enemy. Moreover, due to the convenience of the geography, the undulations of the mountains, and the density of the forests, they managed to survive. Now they are surrounded and blockaded. Domestic assistance is naturally difficult to reach, and foreign transportation is extremely difficult. What they rely on to support themselves now is only their spirit of enduring hardship. The Righteous Army in those three counties only eats one kind of food: cornmeal. When winter comes, there are naturally no vegetables or salt. They lack all other necessities of life. The replenishment of clothing relies entirely on the raw hides of the few wild animals they hunt.

However, they have created several new things themselves. First, they have no paper, but they have pens that have survived and are not broken. When they want to write an order or pass a message, they use the inner husks of corn as paper and barely manage to write. They still want to smoke, but there is no possibility of getting cigarettes. Even ready-made dry tobacco is like a treasure. However, they use kitchen knives or bayonets to cut tobacco leaves into shreds, then wrap them in corn husks and smoke them. Such things can truly be said to be forced to reverse the course of history. However, those involved still believe that they must fight to the end and use their primitive methods to fight to the death with the newly emerging imperialists.

Speaking of how Japan treats the people of the three northeastern provinces, first we must think of the so-called "Manchukuo" taxes. At the beginning of the Japanese invasion of Northeast China, they repeatedly claimed that they were overthrowing warlord rule. Therefore, in the past, many people were anesthetized by them, and many people were willing to be their running dogs, seeking immediate benefits and foolishly hoping for future gains. However, as of now, the facts have gradually become clear. The increase in taxes is indeed progressing day by day. For example, the regular tax and surcharges levied per "tian" (a unit of land area in Northeast China, equivalent to ten mu in Liaoning, each mu being 720 square steps) used to be no more than 7.5 yuan, but now it has increased to 17 or 18 yuan, or even 20 yuan per "tian." Fortunately, the harvest has been very good in the past two years, and they can still barely manage to endure hardship and live their lives.

Secondly, grain prices are low, less than half of what they used to be. The villagers are all complaining bitterly. The grain they want to sell cannot be sold, and the necessities such as clothing that they want to buy cannot be bought. The most difficult thing is the man-made restrictions. Since Japan has brought all the railways under the management of the South Manchuria Railway Company, it has increased the freight rates very high. Red sorghum that sells for only three or four yuan per shi (a unit of dry measure) in the countryside must cost more than ten yuan to transport it to the interior. Such a vicious plan truly leaves the villagers with no way to go.

Thirdly, it is implementing its so-called general control economy. It is conducting a general survey of the lives of the people in all parts of the three northeastern provinces, except for the above-mentioned counties where the power of the Japanese army cannot reach. It is having the county governments notify each district and township to register the population, land, livestock, vehicles, sleds, chickens, dogs, etc., and have each township and district be responsible for the registration. The forms are sent to the county, from the county to the province, and from the province to the headquarters of the Japanese Kwantung Army. In the event of an emergency, it can follow the survey forms, distribute orders to each county, and assign them without any omissions. Truly, no one can escape. Not long ago, horses and vehicles were requisitioned near Changchun and Jilin for the Asahikawa Division's trip to the Greater Khingan Mountains. After being requisitioned, they were never returned. Although it is only considered a preparatory period now, the economic lives of the people in Northeast China are truly completely in the hands of the Japanese. To try to revolt will also require a great deal of effort. (February 9th)

Alarming News of 2,000 British Soldiers Occupying the Yunnan Border 87

Situation Reported by Li Yuegai and Yang Yiqian

British Soldiers Building Roads and Establishing Wireless Telegraphs

Christian Converts Are All Willing Accomplices

Kunming Correspondence: In December of last year, the border of Yunnan, close to Burma, was suddenly invaded by more than 2,000 British soldiers from Burma, showing a great intention to encroach upon our western frontier. The situation suddenly became tense. The following is an urgent record of the report telegraphed by the two supervisors Li Yuegai and Yang Yiqian last month, to show its general situation.

Report by Li Yuegai 88

(1) To the Yunnan Provincial Government: Top Secret. According to reports, a British mining company is currently raising 7.5 million rupees to operate a mine in the undetermined section of the southern border. The road has been opened to Shanglongdu, and the purpose is probably in the Banglong area. It is said that the excavation of the old silver mine is coming to an end, and the other party has long had the intention of moving the site, which was previously handled by the Yibei Dao. This time it is likely to be realized. Although it is not known who is in charge and where, it seems that there is no doubt that the first step is to start from the Banglong area. It has been found that Banglong and Bangkuang are currently under the influence of the Hui Muslim Ma Meiting. Ma's heart is quite outward-looking, and even County Magistrate Ru Zhen of Na County is difficult to influence due to his Hui Muslim background. In the future, the Banglong area may become another lost cause. (Omission) Supervisor Li Yuegai's seal. (2) To the Yunnan Provincial Government: Top Secret. In addition, the Mengding Tusi reported that merchants from Banglong to Meng were suddenly summoned back by Banglong official Xin Dong (presumably Ma Meiting), and none were allowed to stay outside. The actions of the British are somewhat different from previous years. It is not known what their intentions are. We will report again after confirmation. It has been found that no abnormalities have been reported elsewhere along the border. It is undoubtedly the matter presented in the telegraphic dispatch. Supervisor Li Yuegai's seal. (3) To the Yunnan Provincial Government: Top Secret. They also recruited a large number of horse caravans to carry mining equipment, and are currently actively proceeding. The heads of the various Hululu Wang areas are extremely alarmed by this move. It is now heard that they have summoned more than 1,000 Kawa soldiers to prepare for resistance, and the situation is tense. (Omission) Supervisor Li Yuegai's seal.

The West Route Army Captures Yongxin 91

Bandit Xiao Flees to Fenyi and Suichuan

Provincial Government Appoints Zhou Guixun as County Magistrate

Nanchang Correspondence: Yongxin County, Jiangxi Province, is located at the foot of the famous bandit lair Jinggang Mountain, bordering the counties of Chaling and Youxian in Hunan, and Ninggang, Suichuan, and Lianhua in the bandit-affected area of Jiangxi Province. Due to the overlapping mountains, wilderness, and remoteness, it was occupied by local bandits Wang Zuo and Yuan Wencai in 1927. Later, the Communist bandits Zhu De and Mao Zedong entered Jiangxi from Hunan and Guangdong, and used this as their base. In 1929, the National Army repeatedly launched suppression campaigns, gaining and losing territory in turn. Since then, it has never seen the light of day, and is like a region outside of civilization. Last year, He Jian led the Western Route Army to capture Yongxin and Ninggang. However, Yongxin was too deeply banditized, and transportation was blocked, making it impossible to manage effectively, resulting in the loss of territory. The headquarters of the bandit leader Xiao Ke's pseudo-Eighth Army, the headquarters of the pseudo-Hunan-Jiangxi Military Region, the pseudo-Hunan-Jiangxi Provincial Government, and the pseudo-Red Army School were all located there, no less than a small Moscow in western Jiangxi. In order to eliminate the Red bandit base, He Jian ordered Liu Jianxu to lead the divisions of Chen Guangzhong and Wang Dongyuan to attack Yongxin from Ninggang and Lianhua in November last year, taking a step-by-step approach, building a site and constructing fortifications, gradually advancing. By this year, the strategic locations near Yongxin and the Red bandit fortifications have all been occupied by Liu's troops, pressing towards Yongxin County. The pseudo-Seventeenth and Eighteenth Divisions of the bandit Xiao fled in two routes to Fenyi and Suichuan in the north and south. Only the pseudo-local bandit army held on to their old nest. Military news was recently received that the Chen and Wang divisions of Liu's troops have recovered Yongxin County. The provincial government has appointed Zhou Guixun as the county magistrate to carry out the aftermath.

Xu, He, Kong, and Wu Bandits Daily Approaching Demise 92

Xu Bandit Trapped in Tongba, He Bandit Fled Back to Sangzhi

Henan Bandits Hide in Yangtong, Wu Bandit Retreats to Anhui Territory

Hankou Correspondence: The Xu, He, Kong, and Wu bandits, scattered in the border regions of Shaanxi, Sichuan, Hunan, Hubei, Henan, and Anhui, have apparently formed four major strongholds. After long-term and relentless suppression by the National Army, they all show signs of gradually declining. Among them, the Xu bandit faction developed the fastest in the past year, occupying more than ten counties in Shaanxi and Sichuan, and establishing the "Sichuan-Shaanxi Soviet Government" in Changchi, Nanjiang, presided over by the bogus chairman Zhang Guotao and bogus director of the General Political Department Fu Zhong. The strength of the bandit army also expanded from more than 10,000 to 50,000 or 60,000, including the Fourth, Ninth, Twenty-fifth, Thirtieth, and Thirty-first Armies, as well as independent divisions and the North Sichuan Guerrilla Force. He Wei, Yu Haizhou, Wang Shusheng, and Li Tai served as army commanders, while Wang Hongkun, Ni Zhiliang, Ren Huizhang, and others served as division commanders, all under the banner of the so-called "Fourth Front Army of the Workers and Peasants' Red Army," led by the bogus commander-in-chief Xu Xiangqian, bogus deputy commander-in-chief Wang Shusheng, and bogus director of the Political Department Chen Changhao. There was a growing trend of sweeping across Sichuan. However, after the general offensive by the Sichuan Army, Yingshan, Yilong, Suiding, and Xuanhan were successively recovered by the National Army. The area occupied by the bandits gradually decreased, and their strength also gradually declined. They then attempted to hold the Tongnan-Ba line. Xu Xiangqian personally led the bogus Ninth Army to garrison Tongjiang, Chen Changhao led the bogus Fourth Army to garrison Bazhong, while the Twenty-fifth and Thirty-first Armies garrisoned Nanjiang, and the Thirtieth Army garrisoned Chengkou, thus forming the current situation of encirclement and suppression by various armies. Currently, the First and Second Routes of Liu Xiang's troops are attacking Nanjiang from Zhaoguang, the Third and Fourth Routes are attacking Bazhong from Yilong, and the Fifth and Sixth Routes are attacking Tongjiang from Xuanwan, cutting off the bandit's connection between Sichuan and Shaanxi in the north. Although the Shaanxi Army has not yet moved out, it has all been concentrated and prepared. In the future, descending south along the Han River, they can directly strike the bandit's rear. According to reports from Sichuan, Nanjiang has already been recovered by the National Army. If this information is confirmed, the bandit's situation will become even more precarious, and their attempt to flee to Shaanxi will also be impossible. The He bandit faction, known as the bogus Second Front Army, is operating in the so-called West Hubei Military Region, with He as the commander-in-chief, commanding the Seventh, Eighth, Ninth, and Third Divisions, with Xia Xi and others serving as division commanders. Initially, they invaded Qianjiang County in eastern Sichuan. After their failure, they fled back to Lichuan, Enshi, Yien, Xianfeng, Laifeng, and Hefeng Counties in Hubei Province. Due to the blocking by Xu Yuanquan's army, they fled further towards Sangzhi, Longshan, and Yongshun in western Hunan. It is now reported that they have reached Sangzhi. This place is the hometown of the He bandit and has long been their old base. He Jian is currently dispatching troops to attack them fiercely. The so-called leaders of the Hunan-Hubei bogus government, besides Xia Xi and He Long, include Guan Xiangying, Song Panming, Lu Dongsheng, and Chen Peiyin, who have either been massacred or dispersed. The bandits in southern Hubei are under the command of Kong Hechong, with a so-called Southeast Government. The bandit leader Zhang Tao serves as the bogus chairman and commander-in-chief, and Ye Jinbo serves as the deputy commander. They have the bogus Third Division, the North Jiangxi Division, and the Independent Division, totaling more than 5,000 people. They have repeatedly attacked the Hunan-Hubei Railway and twice invaded Chongyang and Tongshan, but both attempts failed, resulting in significant losses in strength. Three division commanders have already been eliminated. Currently, there are still scattered bandits in Yangxin and Tongshan, and Chen Jicheng is directing the stationed troops to search and suppress them. As for the Wu Huanxian bandit faction, they roam the borders of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui, in the so-called Eastern Hubei Military Region. The original Twenty-fifth and Twenty-eighth Armies, after suffering losses, have been merged into one army, with Wu serving as the army commander and Xu Haidong and Zhou Xiyuan serving as division commanders. It has become difficult for them to gain a foothold in Huang'an and Macheng in eastern Hubei, as well as Guangshan, Luoshan, Shangcheng, and Gushi in southern Henan. It is reported that the remnants of the bandits have now fled into Lihuang County in Anhui Province, where they are exhausted and running out of resources, and are no longer a threat to the three provinces. In summary, these four factions, at their peak, had a total of more than 85,000 people and 50,000 to 60,000 guns. Now, they have lost more than half of their strength. If a large army continues to be deployed against them, regardless of territorial boundaries, the day of complete eradication will not be far off. It is also reported that the Communist bandits held a meeting in Jiangxi, and Article 3 of Item C stated: "The overall situation in the southeast is primarily focused on Hubei Province. Capturing Hubei Province can control Jiangsu and Anhui. Jiangxi Province can serve as a shield. The Red Armies of Sichuan, Shaanxi, Anhui, Hunan, and Jiangxi Provinces should select elite troops and develop towards the Hubei area in multiple routes, coordinating with each other and using guerrilla warfare to expand the Soviet areas. The resolution is to unite the provinces and act simultaneously, so that the National Army cannot deploy troops everywhere, in order to achieve the effect of encirclement." However, the Second National Soviet Congress convened by the bandits in Jiangxi was held on December 11th of last year. At that time, the Fujian rebellion was breaking out, and the overall situation was serious. The military plan of the bandit party was determined in response to the situation at the time. Now, the Fujian rebellion has been quelled, the exit route for the Jiangxi bandits has been cut off, and the Xu, He, Kong, and Wu factions are declining daily. The original plan to "capture Hubei Province" and "develop towards the Hubei area" is absolutely impossible and nothing but a futile dream. (February 19th)

Fuzhou Celebrates Central Army Victory 93

A Touch of the Lunar New Year

A General Overview of Finance, Military Affairs, and Civil Administration

Fuzhou Correspondence: During the Gregorian New Year, Fujian was still under the rule of the bogus People's Government. The bogus Cultural Committee held a so-called "Production and People's Entertainment Conference" at the Chengtian Theater. Fearing bombing by Central aircraft, the opening was held at night. Unexpectedly, only a little more than a month later, during the Lunar New Year, the bogus People's Government completely collapsed. Fujian was restored to the Central Government. All sectors in the provincial capital held a recreational gathering in West Lake Park on February 15th and 16th to celebrate the victory of the Central Army. There were new dramas, old dramas, movies, songs and dances, storytelling, magic, martial arts, dragon lanterns, fireworks, and other activities. Aircraft distributed leaflets, and personnel from the party, government, and military sectors gave speeches. The audience was quite lively. This was indeed a touch of the Lunar New Year.

In terms of finance, the new salaries of various agencies and organizations were paid at one-third of the February and March salaries during the Lunar New Year. However, education expenses were paid at 50%, and teachers and staff were still dissatisfied. They plan to hold another meeting in the coming days to discuss methods of demanding payment. The business and financial situation is also very difficult. Only less than half of the accounts are being paid on the market. Loans from money houses have been extended to the second day of the Lunar New Year. Therefore, no bankruptcies have occurred yet.

In terms of military affairs, news of bandit suppression in northern Fujian is quite quiet. However, according to refugees who escaped from the bandit-occupied counties, the Red bandits are now confiscating military equipment and food obtained from Shunchang, Jiangle, Shaxian, and Yong'an Counties and forcing thousands of laborers to transport them to the bogus army headquarters in Mingxi County for storage. On the other hand, they are promoting heresies, oppressing good people to become Red Guards, and women to become comfort corps. City walls have been demolished, and many people who have been killed are abandoned in the wilderness and mountain pits, which is a very tragic situation. It is reported that after Chiang Ting-wen goes to Quanzhou to assume the post of commander-in-chief of the East Route Army, Wei Lihuang will go to Yanping to assume the post of forward commander of the East Route Army to oversee the bandit suppression efforts.

In terms of civil administration, there has been no significant news in the past week. However, the director of the Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau was replaced by Li Zhengde (from Zhejiang) on the 15th. Sun Jiazhe, the director of the Finance Department, is expected to arrive in Fujian from Shanghai on the 17th. After Sun takes office, Xu Fu will abolish the Finance Special Commissioner's Office, and he plans to go to Nanjing. (Although Xu was recommended by the Provincial Committee as acting director of finance, he still acts in the name of the Finance Special Commissioner to the outside world.) In addition, Li Zuyu, the director of the Civil Affairs Department, is expected to come to Fujian to take office during the Lantern Festival in the Lunar New Year. The Security Office began operations on the 16th and is attached to the Provincial Government, with Chen Yi concurrently serving as the director, Xiao Qian serving as the deputy director, and Chen Jingcun serving as the chief of staff. The future powers of this office will be quite significant. All troops not belonging to the East Route Bandit Suppression Army will be under the jurisdiction of this office, in order to increase the power of the Provincial Chairman in politics.

In terms of party affairs, the current situation is being temporarily maintained by Party Affairs Special Commissioner Dai Kuisheng, and no progress is being made, pending the arrival of the newly appointed Special Commissioner Chen Zhaoying to take over. (February 17th)

Chiang Cables Hubei Provincial Government Reaffirming Opium Planting Ban 94

And Stopping Military and Government Agencies from Harassing and Extorting

Hankou Correspondence: Chairman Chiang, considering that western and northern Hubei often violate the ban on opium planting, which urgently needs to be thoroughly eradicated, cabled the Hubei Provincial Government again on the 17th, reaffirming the ban and ordering strict prohibition of planting. Violators will be severely punished in accordance with the repeated orders. Furthermore, considering that the stationed troops and local officials and gentry in western and northern Hubei are arbitrarily increasing special taxes and surcharges, or harassing and extorting, he also cabled Zhang Qun, Qian Dajun, and Xu Yuanquan to investigate and prohibit it. The cable reads: "Chairman Zhang of Wuchang, Chief of Staff Qian of the General Headquarters, and forwarding to Commander-in-Chief Xu, as well as all division commanders and Director Huang of the Special Tax Office: Recently, it has been reported that the stationed troops, and local officials and gentry in western and northern Hubei are still arbitrarily collecting special taxes and surcharges, or harassing and extorting under various pretexts, which is a clear violation of discipline and extremely hateful. It is hoped that you will separately and earnestly investigate and prohibit it, and instruct all military and government personnel and local leaders under your command to strictly comply. If it is found again that anyone arbitrarily extorts or harasses and extorts, they will be severely punished, and the responsible officials will not be able to evade their responsibilities. You must comply with this and report back for further action. Chiang Kai-shek's seal, Jiangxi," (February 19th)

Songjiang

Record of the Standing Committee Meeting of the River Dredging Committee 95

The River Dredging Committee established its office in the Quan Jie Tang today (the 20th). All department staff members reported for duty and began work. The committee also held its second standing committee meeting. County Magistrate Jin Tigan, the chairman, performed the rituals and reported on the progress of preparations. Then, they discussed the proposals, the main points of which were: (1) Regarding the case of discussing and determining the location for dumping mud during the dredging of the city river, it was resolved that the directors of each section should investigate and determine the locations for dumping mud within their jurisdiction and report them to the standing committee members for verification. (2) The estimated cost of dredging the river in this session, including the tributaries, is 63,000 yuan. In addition to the 28,000 yuan allocated by the official authorities, there is still a shortage of 35,000 yuan. How should we raise the money locally? It was resolved that fundraising should be divided into two types: general and special. The general donation will be based on the example of the house rent donation collected last year. For houses that are residential or self-owned and do not have a rental price to base on, the value will be estimated and determined. Special donations will be levied on industries such as bamboo and wood, rice, knitting, and coarse paper making. Donation tickets will be divided into red and black to show the difference. (3) Regarding the case of adding Hutxi River to the list of tributaries to be dredged, it was resolved that it be passed.

The Guns of the Security Corps Were Robbed 96

The headquarters of the Chenjiaxing Winter Defense Security Corps was suddenly attacked by a number of bandits late on the 18th. They encountered the corps police and clashed. However, they were outnumbered and outgunned. As a result, the bandits robbed two rifles and left in a hurry. The director of the corps has reported the incident to the county police authorities, requesting them to pursue and arrest the thieves and recover the stolen goods in order to deter illegal activities. Suzhou

The Construction Department Hastens to Build the Suchang Road 97

Among the three highways with Suzhou as the center, namely the Sujia, Sukun, and Suchang Roads, the Sujia Road has been fully opened to traffic, and the Sukun Road has also completed the roadbed. Only the Changshu section of the Suchang Road has completed the roadbed. Now, the Jiangsu Construction Department has determined that these three roads must be completed before the opening of the Southeast Transportation Exhibition to be held in June. It has specially dispatched engineer Wen Zhengwei, who came to Suzhou yesterday (the 20th) to work with technical director Zhou Jun and surveyor Hua Chi to inspect the construction methods of the Suchang Road. As a result, it was decided that the road would be connected to the Suzhou Ring Road outside the railway station at Yangqi to connect with the Sujia Road. It was also decided that all road work would be rushed to completion within two months. The entire road requires the construction of 24 bridges, which will be planned by the department and then constructed. In the future, the road can reach Suzhou from Changshu, and then to Jiaxing in Zhejiang Province, or directly to Shanghai via the Sukun Road.

Dredging the Wusong River Can Be Realized 98

The Taihu Lake Basin Water Conservancy Committee, the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce, and others petitioned the central government to allocate cotton and wheat loans to dredge the Wusong River. According to the latest news from the Taihu Lake Water Conservancy Committee, the case has been resolved by the Central Political Conference. All water conservancy matters will be handled by the National Economic Committee in a unified manner, and a portion of the cotton and wheat loans will be allocated for construction. The National Economic Committee is currently planning this, and the issue of dredging the Wusong River is likely to be realized.

Wuxi

The County Chamber of Commerce Schedules Reorganization 99

After the second election of the County Chamber of Commerce on January 15th, a dispute arose because the incumbent supervisory committee member was elected as an executive committee member. An interpretation was requested from the Ministry of Industry and Commerce. The Ministry replied by telegram, stating that the incumbent supervisory committee member only needed to resign and be appointed as an executive committee member. Due to the end of the lunar year, reorganization could not be completed. Therefore, yesterday (the 20th) at noon, after holding a spring banquet at the chamber, a tea party was held. Chairman Yang Hanxi discussed the cases: (1) The second executive committee will hold a meeting within February 25th to reorganize and elect standing committee members. (2) Regarding the issue of brokerage licenses, a meeting of the relevant industries will be held on a scheduled basis to discuss a solution. (3) The construction of houses next to the chamber will be handled by the executive committee after the design is completed. After discussing academic matters, the meeting adjourned.

The Total Number of Rice Stored in Warehouses 100

Our county is known as a rice-gathering area. Rice merchants from various provinces come to Wuxi to buy and sell, mainly because Wuxi's land and water transportation are more convenient, and warehouses are lined up. In recent years, there have been bumper harvests, but sales have been sluggish, and all warehouses are overflowing. At the beginning of last winter, because there were many soybeans, the warehouse space was already tight when rice and paddy were on the market. By the end of the accounting period, all warehouses were full, which was more than the previous year. The inventory of each warehouse is as follows: 631,100 dan of japonica paddy, 139,800 dan of yuan paddy, 827,200 dan of indica paddy, 1,100 shi of unpolished yuan rice, 224,000 shi of unpolished japonica rice, 33,100 shi of unpolished indica rice, 27,700 shi of wheat, 398,800 shi of soybeans, 98,100 shi of mung beans, and 77,600 shi of miscellaneous grains. Rice merchants, rice mills, and rice shops opened yesterday, and the tea party for the rice industry set the market price for unpolished japonica rice, which was one jiao higher than last year, while japonica paddy was five fen higher, white rice was one or two jiao higher, and white indica rice was two jiao higher. The rest also increased slightly. The prices are: 6.1 jiao to 5.4 jiao for unpolished japonica rice, 6.5 jiao to 5.9 jiao for unpolished yuan rice, 5.4 jiao to 5.1 jiao for unpolished Dazi rice, 5.7 jiao to 5.3 jiao for unpolished Yangxian rice, 3.15 jiao to 3.0 jiao for japonica paddy, 2.95 jiao to 2.6 jiao for Dazi paddy, 3.1 jiao to 2.9 jiao for Yangxian paddy, 3.5 jiao to 3.3 jiao for yuan paddy, 6.9 jiao to 6.0 jiao for white rice, 6.5 jiao to 5.8 jiao for white Yangxian rice, 4.6 jiao for wheat, 2.5 jiao to 2.1 jiao for barley, and 5.0 jiao for soybeans.

Provincial Order to Thoroughly Investigate Bribery and Connivance with Opium Traffickers 101

The county government of our district recently received an order from the Jiangsu Provincial Government to thoroughly investigate whether Yao Chunjie, the former chief of the special affairs team of the Wuxi Public Security Bureau, had colluded with Liu Yueqing, the chief of the Ninth Branch Bureau, to privately release Yu Zhu, an opium trafficker from Zhuxiang Lane, Kaiyuan Township (i.e., the wife of Yu Shengqing), in exchange for a bribe. Furthermore, the 63 taels of opium, 45 yuan in silver dollars, and 55 yuan in paper money seized at the scene were not handed over to the authorities. In addition, Cai Yulong handled 200 yuan in silver dollars as a condition for avoiding arrest. If this is true, they should be severely punished. After receiving the order, County Magistrate Yan ordered the Public Security Bureau yesterday to start the investigation in order to verify the facts.

Zhenjiang

The Construction Bureau Will Be Established at the Beginning of the Month 102

The construction bureaus of the counties in Jiangsu Province were abolished last year due to financial difficulties. Shen Baixian, the current director of the Construction Department, believes that it is necessary to restore construction in the important counties north and south of the Yangtze River. Therefore, the departments in Zhenjiang, Wuxi, Wuxian, Baoshan, Nantong, and Rugao are being converted into bureaus. The bureau chiefs have been appointed separately. Liu Yongnian, the bureau chief of Zhenjiang Construction Bureau, came to the province yesterday to visit Director Shen and ask for instructions on everything. It is reported that the Zhenjiang bureau will be restored on March 1st. The internal organization is simple. Under the bureau chief, there will only be two sections: administrative affairs and technology. Each section will have one director, and below them will only be one administrative and one technical staff member.

Yangzhou

A General Overview of Various Industries After the Year-End Accounting 103

In Yangzhou, less than 50% of the stores, following the usual practice, reopened on the 18th (i.e., the day of the God of Wealth in the lunar calendar) after the year-end accounting for the 22nd year. Very few made a profit, mainly due to the impact of rural bankruptcy. A survey of the conditions of various industries is as follows: The money industry has declined since the abolition of taels and the change to yuan. Among the accounting statements of various banks, Yisheng Bank showed a slightly larger profit, but it was still less than 10,000 yuan, which was far from previous years. Yesterday, the colleagues gathered and discussed a plan to reopen on the 20th. The original banks, such as Hongda and Hengchang, have decided to close down. Yuanchang has not yet made a decision. Shengyuan has changed its bank name to Dachang. The other banks, such as Huichangyong, Huiyu, Baoxing, Chengzhang, Yisheng, Hengda, and Shengyu, are expected to reopen on time. The silk and cloth industries were affected by mutual price competition last year. After accounting, they could only barely cover expenses and did not have much profit. Apart from Hongxingtiansun Jin and other shops that had already closed down at the end of the year, it is now reported that Tianxiang Silk Shop is also struggling to survive. Hongda has not yet made a decision. Among the cloth industry, Chunhe, Yukang, and Yuanda have not been able to reopen. The others are expected to operate as usual. Guanghuo, Gu embroidery, and perfume, etc., have had difficulty maintaining operations due to sluggish business. They have all reduced the number of employees and tightened expenses. Although the rice, firewood, and food industries were affected by the low price of grain, they were still able to make a profit. As for silver shops, shoe stores, hat shops, copper and tin shops, and pharmacies, they mostly lost money.

Changzhou

Opening of the Industrial Joint Exhibition 104

The Wujin Branch of the China Industrial Federation, in order to promote the use of domestic goods, specially organized the Wujin Industrial Joint Exhibition. In the early stages, it collected products from various factories and sent them to the exhibition for display. After a long period of preparation, the opening ceremony was held at the County Chamber of Commerce at 2:00 PM on the 19th. The exhibition venue was located in the First Park. There were more than 20 participating manufacturers selling more than 30 categories of goods, such as silk and cloth, enamel, toothbrushes, and leather goods. In addition, there were more than 50 manufacturers displaying items. Local residents and representatives of various agencies and organizations went to participate, and the crowd was unusually large. The association also marked, "Not using domestic goods is tantamount to suicide, and loving foreign goods is equivalent to betraying the country" as the purpose of the meeting, which was quite alarming.

The Security Corps in Nantong, Pingchao, Xingren, and other districts caused trouble by shooting and killing villagers while collecting land donations. The Jiaxing County Chamber of Commerce, believing that the heavy land tax surcharges in the county have had a significant impact on the business market, has cabled various ministries and provincial and county authorities, requesting a reduction and exemption in order to alleviate the difficulties of farmers. The Memorial Service for the King of Belgium Will Be Held in This City Next Monday 109

The National Government Issued a Circular Yesterday to Fly Flags at Half-Mast for Three Days

Minister to Belgium, Mr. Jules de Laminne, Will Come in Person to Preside

The Location Is the Catholic Church on Catholic Church Street

After the passing of King Albert of Belgium, the world was shocked and mourned. Ambassadors and consuls from various countries in this city, as well as relevant foreign affairs officials from our country, went to the Belgian Consulate General to offer condolences and fly flags at half-mast for three days. Mr. Jules de Laminne, the Belgian Minister to China, will leave Beijing for Shanghai this week and will hold a grand memorial service at the Catholic Church on Catholic Church Street in the French Concession on the 26th (Monday). Diplomatic agencies in our country, as well as ambassadors and consuls from various countries in China, and naval generals stationed in China will all attend the Catholic Church at that time. The details are recorded as follows:

National Government Circular Expressing Condolences 110

Chairman Lin Sen of the National Government and Premier Wang Jingwei issued a circular to all national agencies yesterday for the passing of the King of Belgium, stating that all government agencies in the country should fly flags at half-mast for three days starting from the 20th of this month to express condolences. You are to comply with this and instruct your subordinates to comply as well.

Belgian Minister Schedules Memorial Service 111

The Belgian Minister Plenipotentiary to China, Baron Jules de Laminne, in order to commemorate the late King Albert I of Belgium, has specifically scheduled a memorial service at the St. Joseph's Cathedral on Catholic Church Street in the French Concession at 11:30 AM on the 26th of this month to comfort his soul. If any groups or ladies and gentlemen from all walks of life intend to participate in the memorial service at that time, they should contact the Belgian Embassy at 1300 Lafayette Road in this city as soon as possible in order to reserve seats.

The Municipal Council Offered Condolences Yesterday 112

Since the tragic death of the King of Belgium, the Public Concession Municipal Council in the Public Concession specially raised flags at half-mast yesterday to express condolences. Director General Mr. Bair also sent a letter to the Acting Consul General of Belgium in Shanghai, on behalf of the Municipal Council, to express his deep condolences to the Belgian Consulate and the Belgian community. The King of Belgium's great achievements and virtues are loved by all. It is understandable that his subjects are deeply saddened by this tragic event.

General Li Du's Speech 113

The Central Government Sent Li to Xinjiang, Li Only Saw the News in the Papers

Two Methods Have Been Sought to Settle Dependents

According to the Guowen News Agency, Li Du, the Commander-in-Chief of the Northeast Anti-Japanese Jilin Self-Defense Army, went to Tianjin to visit relatives. Now that he has finished his business, he arrived in Shanghai from Beijing by the night train the night before last and returned to his residence. Yesterday afternoon at 4:00 PM, Wu Huanzhang, the representative of Ma Zhanshan, went to his residence to visit Li and had a conversation. The reporter went to visit, but Wu had just left. The following conversation was held with Mr. Li:

Complex Internal Situation in Xinjiang 114

Li said, "I am from Shenyang, but I haven't been to Tianjin for several years, so I took the opportunity to go there. The trip took five days. Because time was tight, I did not meet with anyone except for handling personal matters in Tianjin. Therefore, General Ma (Zhanshan) also did not go to visit. The situation in Xinjiang is complicated. I only saw the news in the papers about the Central Government sending me to Xinjiang to reorganize the old troops. Therefore, I don't know anything in detail. If the Central Government orders, we soldiers will not hesitate to go through fire and water. However, Xinjiang is a barren land, and the overland route from Gansu to Dihua alone is more than 4,000 li, which takes more than 40 days. News is also isolated and difficult to communicate. Sheng Shicai, the chairman, had about 2,000 troops when he first entered Xinjiang. Now he governs the three major commercial ports of Dihua, Tacheng, and Yili. Ma Zhongying is a Hui Muslim army with about 4,000 troops. Ma's strength is like the Northeast Volunteer Army. They are all local Hui Muslims who have joined. Among those who possess this strength in Xinjiang, the old troops from Jilin are about 8,000. Their livelihood, apart from rations, can be said to have no regular salary at all. Therefore, they are extremely distressed and have no other hope. They all hope that the Central Government can quickly formally reorganize them. Currently, the commanding officers in Xinjiang include Brigade Commander Zheng Runcheng, as well as Xing Zhanqing, Wang Xiaoxian, Gong Yinqing, and Hou Zhanbin. It is heard that the Central Government has sent Minister Huang to Xinjiang, which is probably true. I passed through Beijing twice but did not visit Premier Wang."

Methods for Settling Dependents 115

As for the officials and officers' dependents who previously transited through Russia to return to China, they are currently scattered in Tianjin, Shanghai, Ping [Beijing], and other places, numbering approximately 300. Their daily sustenance is quite difficult. I believe that those who are unable to feel at ease are precisely this group of helpless dependents. In the past, their maintenance relied on donations from various parties. Initially, the Central Party Headquarters in the capital collected over 40,000 yuan in donations. Subsequently, Mr. Wang Xiaolai and others in this city also contributed over 10,000 yuan. Recently, Deputy Commander Zhang (Xueliang) also allocated 5,000 yuan as maintenance funds for the dependents. Since their return to the country, a total of over 70,000 yuan has been spent. Since being forced to come to Shanghai, I have no possessions. If the dependents continue to drift about like this, their future livelihoods are quite worrying. Therefore, I have recently found several solutions: first, to provide financial assistance to the dependents to go to Xinjiang, so that wives, children, and fathers can be reunited; second, to enable the old troops to be reorganized by the central government, so that men can earn money and the dependents can support themselves. This matter is currently being vigorously pursued. My recent stay in Shanghai is not related to the attempted assassination of General Ma. The incident occurred after I had already left Tianjin en route, so I am completely unaware of the details. After speaking, he bid farewell and departed.

New Shanghai-Peiping Passenger Train Completed for the Shanghai-Nanjing Railway 116

The Trial Run at the Zha Kou Yesterday Morning Yielded Excellent Results

All Circles to be Invited to Visit at the North Station Tomorrow

After the Shanghai-Peiping through transport was implemented, the Shanghai-Nanjing Railway specially commissioned the Wusong Machinery Factory to rush to build a Shanghai-Peiping through train. Before it was completed, it was temporarily borrowed from the Beining and Huning Railways. Now that it has been completed, it was driven to the Zha Kou yesterday for a trial run, with excellent results. Tomorrow, all circles will be invited to visit. Details are noted below.

Completion of Trial Run 117

After the Shanghai-Peiping through train of the Shanghai-Nanjing Railway was completed and modified, it included two first-class sleeper cars, three second-class sleeper cars, three third-class passenger cars, one dining car, one lounge car, and one baggage car, totaling eleven cars. It departed from Shanghai North Station at 8:10 a.m. yesterday for the Zha Kou Station of the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway for a trial run. Yang Xianfen, section chief specially appointed by the Business Department of the Ministry of Railways, came to inspect. Zheng Baozhao, director of the Transportation Department, Wang Zhigang, chief of the Transportation Section, and Mo Heng, director of the General Affairs Department, all accompanied the train to Hangzhou. Due to the need to protect the passenger cars along the way, it did not arrive at Zha Kou Station until 4:19 p.m., with excellent results. It departed for Shanghai at 5:30 p.m. and arrived at Shanghai North Station at around 10:00 p.m.

Invitation to Visit 118

After the completion of the new Shanghai-Peiping through train by the Lianglu Administration [Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway Administrations], all circles will be invited to visit tomorrow. Invitation cards have already been distributed yesterday, saying, "The Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administration of the Shanghai-Nanjing Railway cordially invites you to visit and provide guidance on the new Shanghai-Peiping through passenger train of this railway at Shanghai North Station at 10:00 a.m. on Thursday, February 22nd. Respectfully ordered, Huang Boqiao and Wu Shaozeng."
