Small Knowledge

Common Knowledge of the Calendar 219

— Bingyu

We commonly use two types of calendars, the solar and lunar calendars, to calculate years, months, and days. (1) The solar calendar, also known as the sun calendar, is compiled according to the tropical year. In other words, it is based on the apparent motion of the sun (determined by the time it takes for the sun to complete one revolution as observed from Earth). One tropical year is approximately 365.2422 days. For practical purposes, a common year is set at 365 days and a leap year at 366 days. Therefore, the fractional part of the tropical year is multiplied by four, resulting in approximately 0.9688 days. This is why there is a leap year after every three common years. However, there are still excesses and deficiencies, as it is not a perfectly precise number. Calculating it this way still leaves a very small remainder. After 400 years, there is a remainder of 3.12 days, meaning that after 100, 200, or 300 years, a leap year must be skipped to compensate. (For example, a year divisible by four in the Western calendar is a leap year, but a year divisible by 100 cannot be divided by four again, making it a common year.) (2) The months in the solar calendar are of varying lengths. Months one, three, five, seven, eight, ten, and twelve are all long months with 31 days, while months four, six, nine, and eleven are short months with 30 days. February has 28 days in a common year and 29 days in a leap year, making February a short-short month. This is due to the continuation of the incomplete calendar from the time of the ancient Roman King Numa Pompilius and does not have any particular deep meaning. (3) The lunar calendar is calculated based on the phases of the moon. There are two methods: the first focuses solely on the waxing and waning of the moon and is called the pure lunar calendar; the second takes into account the changes in climate caused by the sun's movement and is known as the lunisolar calendar. The first type is used in the Islamic calendar, and the second is used in the Chinese calendar, also known as the Greek calendar. The waxing and waning of the moon takes approximately 29.5306 days, so twelve months have approximately 354.367 days. Therefore, the lunar calendar has 354 or 355 days in a year, which is eleven days shorter than the tropical year of 365 days. This means that in less than three years, it is short by 30 days. Thus, there is a leap month every two years to adjust for the tropical year. (4) Each of the four seasons, spring, summer, autumn, and winter, has six solar terms. Although most people know the names of these twenty-four solar terms, many do not understand the meaning of each term. Now, I will briefly explain each solar term. Lichun (立春) signifies the beginning of spring. Yushui (雨水) signifies that ice and snow turn into rainwater. Jingzhe (驚蟄) signifies that insects hibernating underground are about to crawl onto the ground. Chunfen (春分) signifies the middle of spring when day and night are of equal length. Qingming (清明) signifies that trees and plants grow branches and leaves. Guyu (穀雨) signifies the nourishment of all grains (the above are the six solar terms of spring). Lixia (立夏) signifies the initial arrival of summer. Xiaoman (小滿) signifies that all things are gradually becoming full. Mangzhong (芒種) signifies the time for planting awned grains. Xiazhi (夏至) signifies the peak of summer, when the days are longest. Xiaoshu (小暑) signifies the beginning of hot weather. Dashu (大暑) signifies the peak of hot weather (the above are the six solar terms of summer). Liqiu (立秋) signifies the initial arrival of autumn. Chushu (處暑) signifies the retreat of hot weather. Bailu (白露) signifies the season when dew falls. Qiufen (秋分) signifies the middle of autumn, when day and night are of equal length. Hanlu (寒露) signifies that the cold is increasing daily. Shuangjiang (霜降) signifies that dew turns into frost (the above are the six solar terms of autumn). Lidong (立冬) signifies the arrival of winter. Xiaoxue (小雪) signifies that rainwater condenses into snow. Daxue (大雪) signifies that it often snows. Dongzhi (冬至) signifies the peak of winter, when the days are shortest. Xiaohan (小寒) signifies that the cold is slightly intense. Dahan (大寒) signifies that it feels very cold. (5) Jiefen (節分) refers to the day divided by the winter and spring solar terms of the lunar calendar, which is the day before Lichun. Rumei (入梅) refers to the day of entering the plum rain season, which is when the sun reaches 80 degrees of ecliptic longitude (with the vernal equinox as the starting point, evenly dividing the ecliptic into 360 degrees) six days after Mangzhong. Banxia Sheng (半夏生) refers to the time when the medicinal herb Banxia grows, which is when the sun reaches 100 degrees of ecliptic longitude. (6) The practice of assigning the seven luminaries, the sun, moon, Mars, Mercury, Jupiter, Venus, and Saturn, to the days within a week, such as the moon for Monday, Mars for Tuesday, and Mercury for Wednesday, was first created by the astrologers of Chaldea in Judea 2,300 years ago. (7) Lunar phases have been inherited for thousands of years. The shape of the moon can be used to determine the date within a month. For example, Shuo (朔) is the new moon, Wang (望) is the full moon, the 7th and 8th are the first quarter moon, and the 22nd and 23rd are the last quarter moon. (8) A solar eclipse occurs during the new moon, when the moon blocks the sun's surface, preventing sunlight from reaching the Earth. There are total eclipses, annular eclipses, and partial eclipses. A lunar eclipse occurs during the full moon because the Earth blocks the sun's surface, preventing sunlight from reaching the moon. The above is some common knowledge about the calendar. It may seem simple, but nine out of ten people in society do not understand it.

The Assault on Shen Huichun

Sports News: The District Court Prosecutor Files Charges 220

Defendant Qin Shaoji Actually Committed the Crime of Assault

The Court's Criminal Division Will Hold a Hearing This Morning at 10:00 AM

The Referees Association Declines Wang Zhengting's Mediation, Expressing a Firm Stance 221

Mr. Shen Huichun, a famous referee in Shanghai's sports community, was invited last year to referee a football match between National Jinan University and Jiaotong University, organized by the Jiangnan Universities Sports Association. The match, held at Jiaotong University's stadium, was crucial for both schools to win the championship, leading to intense competition. Referees officiating such games face arduous work and require careful judgment, only those with high reputation can handle the task. Mr. Shen Huichun was certainly capable of handling the responsibility, as both schools trusted and hired him. Ultimately, Jiaotong University suffered a narrow defeat by one goal. Students, distraught over losing the championship, had an abrupt change of emotion. A few radical members blamed the referee for unfair decisions and confronted Mr. Shen. A student surnamed Qin, named Shaoji, even used a weapon to violently assault Mr. Shen, who fell to the ground injured and was further attacked by the crowd, suffering severe injuries. Fortunately, Dr. Rong Qizhao, president of the Jiangnan Universities Sports Association, and Ye Peichu of Jinan University, rescued Mr. Shen from the mob and rushed him to Tongren Hospital for treatment. They also submitted a medical report to the Shanghai District Court Prosecutor's Office for assessment. Mr. Shen hired lawyer E Sen as his representative to file a criminal complaint against the student Qin Shaoji for assault. Prosecutor Tang Ruxiu of the court held several hearings, and the defendant An Shaoji was released on bail as instructed. These events have been repeatedly reported in this newspaper. It is now known that after a thorough investigation by Prosecutor Tang, he deeply believes that the defendant Qin Shaoji actually committed the crimes specified in Articles 42 and 293, Paragraph 1 of the Criminal Law. Therefore, in accordance with Article 253, Paragraph 1 of the Criminal Law, he has filed a public prosecution against Qin. The court's criminal division has accepted the case and scheduled a hearing for both parties this morning at 10:00 AM. The prosecutor's indictment is copied below:

Indictment by the Prosecutor of the Shanghai District Court 222

Defendant Qin Shaoji, male, 23 years old, from Cixi, residing at 36 F煦 Village, F煦 Road, student.

The above-mentioned case of assault, number 7001 in the investigation of the Republic of China Year 22, has been fully investigated and is deemed suitable for public prosecution. The defendant's criminal facts, reasons for prosecution, and the violated articles of law are listed below:

▲Facts of the Crime Qin Shaoji is a student at Jiaotong University. On the afternoon of December 16th of last year, at 2:30 PM, Jiaotong University and Jinan University competed in football at the Jiaotong University stadium, and Shen Huichun was hired as the referee. When the game resulted in a one-goal defeat for Jiaotong University, Qin Shaoji, angered by the defeat, blamed Shen Huichun for unfair refereeing. At the end of the game, he gathered many unidentified individuals and together they assaulted Shen Huichun, resulting in injuries. A complaint was filed.

Reasons for Prosecution and Violated Articles of Law Upon investigation, it was found that Shen Huichun suffered minor injuries to both his left and right hands, as confirmed by the forensic medical report on file. The injuries to his head and other areas are also supported by the diagnosis from Tongren Hospital. Furthermore, Shen Guoquan, an eyewitness at the time, testified that he saw blood flowing from Shen Huichun's head, which is true. The defendant and many unidentified individuals jointly assaulted Shen Huichun at the end of the game. Not only did Shen Huichun clearly and repeatedly describe the events, but also Lu Xiangqian, Liang Wendong, Chen Bingde, Gao Chengju, and others present at the scene uniformly testified to this effect. It is extremely clear that Shen Huichun's injuries were inflicted by the defendant and others. Moreover, the defendant confessed, "During those few minutes, I was very unhappy because my school's training achievements for the entire semester were ruined." This shows that the defendant was angered by the defeat, and his anger led to the assault, which is undeniably proven. As for the defendant's defense, "At the time, I was standing far away from where he was beaten. I was wearing white clothes, which made me very noticeable. I did not participate in the assault. There are police officers from the sixth district who were maintaining order, as well as Wang Yongzhi, Wu Shutang, and Tu Kaiyuan, who can testify to this," the summoned police officers Meng Dazhao and Zhang Dongming both stated, "During the fight, the crowd was very crowded, and I could not clearly see if anyone wearing white clothes participated in the assault." Furthermore, Wang Yongzhi and Wu Shutang both stated, "When they became crowded, I walked away. I don't know what happened after that." Therefore, the statements of these witnesses are insufficient to prove that the defendant did not commit the assault. Considering that Shen Huichun had no prior grudges against the defendant and would not intentionally frame him, the defendant should undoubtedly be held responsible for the crime of assault. The defendant actually committed the crimes specified in Articles 42 and 293, Paragraph 1 of the Criminal Law. Therefore, in accordance with Article 253, Paragraph 1 of the Criminal Procedure Law, prosecution is initiated. Prosecutor Tang Ruxiu, Clerk Li Yanzhao, February 7th, Republic of China Year 23.

▲Attitude of the Referees Association The entire membership of the Shanghai China Sports Referees Association convened an emergency meeting last night regarding the Shen case, considering it concerns the rise and fall of China's entire sports community and the survival of sportsmanship. The unanimous conclusion was to request the court to severely punish the chief perpetrator of the assault, thoroughly investigate the accomplices, and order compensation for Shen's medical expenses and other losses. If this goal is not achieved, they will determine steps to not cooperate with the Shanghai sports community. If so, all sports events in Shanghai will be in a state of lacking referees. The school authority should take responsibility of this consequence. Furthermore, the association dispatched representatives to attend today's court hearing and requested those who witnessed the incident to testify in court. The association, while expressing gratitude for the mediation efforts of Mr. Wang Zhengting, chairman of the China National Amateur Athletic Federation, respectfully declined the mediation because the case has been formally accepted by the court.

Tilden on America's Failure in the Davis Cup 237

Blames It on Illegal Management

Deeply Regrets Vines

Education News From Other Places

Hunan Elementary School Teacher Dispute: General to Implement Teacher Qualification Examination 239

Changsha Correspondence: Zhu Jingnong, the Director of the Education Department of Hunan Province, issued an order to reorganize the qualifications of elementary school teachers, which caused a major storm in the elementary education sector of the province. Students from normal schools and those from non-normal schools formed two major factions. The non-normal school faction organized the Hunan Elementary School Teachers' Professional Maintenance Association and launched a large-scale petition, demanding that all non-normal school graduates who have been engaged in elementary education for many years and have achieved significant results should be employed. On the other hand, the normal school faction also organized the Hunan Normal School Graduates Association and launched a large-scale petition, supporting the Education Department's order to reorganize the qualifications of elementary school teachers, demanding that no one other than normal school graduates should be employed as elementary school teachers. Both sides were running around, each taking extreme positions. Director Zhu then submitted a request to the Ministry of Education for approval to formulate regulations for elementary school teacher qualification examination in Hunan Province before the central government issues relevant regulations. Those who pass the examination, even if they are not from normal schools, will be allowed to serve as elementary school teachers as a means of relief. However, due to time constraints, it was decided that the examination will be held simultaneously in eleven districts throughout the province during the summer vacation this year, with a budget of over 6,000 yuan. Therefore, prominent figures in the education sector, such as Huang Shiheng (賓步) and Cheng Caozi (谷) and others, came forward to mediate, advocating that the reorganization of elementary school teacher qualifications should be implemented after the summer vacation examination, and that elementary school teachers should not be replaced before the examination. It is not yet known whether Director Zhu of the Education Department will adopt this proposal. If it can be implemented in this way, the current turmoil in the Hunan elementary school sector can be fundamentally resolved. The examination regulations and the organizational regulations of the examination committee are recorded below.

▲ Provisional Regulations for the Elementary School Teacher Qualification Examination of the Education Department of Hunan Province: Article 1: In order to reorganize the qualifications of elementary school teachers and promote the development of elementary schools, the Education Department of Hunan Province, with the approval of the Ministry of Education, will temporarily establish a committee to handle the qualification examination of elementary school teachers throughout the province before the central government's regulations on elementary school teacher qualification examination are promulgated. The organizational regulations of the committee will be separately determined. Article 2: The qualification examination of elementary school teachers is divided into the following two types: (A) Qualification examination without testing: Reviewing various supporting documents (graduation certificates, study certificates, service certificates, works, etc.) to make a decision. (B) Qualification examination with testing: In addition to reviewing various certificates, tests will also be conducted. Article 3: Those who possess one of the following qualifications may be subject to qualification examination without testing: (1) Graduates of old-system middle schools or higher secondary schools, who have served as elementary school teachers for more than one year, or have attended summer schools organized by the Provincial Education Department, university education colleges, or normal schools to make up for education courses for two summer sessions; (2) Graduates of two-year or longer normal training courses, or simplified normal schools or simplified normal departments, who have served as elementary school teachers for more than two years, or have attended the summer schools mentioned in the preceding paragraph to make up for courses for one summer session; (3) Those who have served as elementary school teachers for more than three years and are recognized by the education administrative authorities as having achieved significant results, or have attended the summer schools in the first paragraph to make up for courses for four summer sessions; (4) Those who have served as elementary school teachers for more than three years and have published special works on elementary education, which have been reviewed and recognized by the Education Department as having definite value. Article 4: Those who possess one of the following qualifications may be subject to qualification examination with testing: (1) Graduates of old-system middle schools or higher secondary schools; (2) Those who have studied at normal schools or higher secondary schools for a certain number of years and have served as elementary school teachers for more than one year; (3) Graduates of normal training courses, simplified normal schools, or simplified normal departments; (4) Those who have served as elementary school teachers for more than three years; (5) Those who have specialized skills and have served as elementary school teachers for more than one year. Article 5: Those who have any of the following circumstances may not be subject to any type of qualification examination: (1) Those who have made reactionary remarks or engaged in reactionary behavior that has been verified; (2) Those who have been subject to criminal penalties of imprisonment or above; (3) Those who have improper behavior or bad habits; (4) Those who are physically disabled or have chronic diseases that prevent them from working; (5) Those who have been subject to revocation of their license. Article 6: Qualification examination with testing will be held once a year in different districts. Article 7: The testing subjects for elementary school class teachers are Civics, Hygiene, National Language, Arithmetic, General Knowledge of Social Sciences, General Knowledge of Natural Sciences, Educational Psychology, Principles of Education, School Administration, and Teaching Methods. The level is based on the high school normal school curriculum. Article 8: The testing subjects for elementary school specialized teachers are one or several subjects such as Physical Education, Art, Music, Manual Arts, Hygiene, and Nature, and Principles of Education and Teaching Methods will also be tested. The level is based on the high school normal school curriculum. Article 9: The testing is divided into written examination, oral examination, and practical examination. Article 10: In the qualification examination with testing, the average score of each subject must be 60 points or above, and each subject must be 50 points or above to pass. Article 11: Those who pass the qualification examination for elementary school teachers will be issued a license by the Education Department. Article 12: A fee of one dime must be paid when receiving the license. Article 13: If there is any change of name, damage, or loss after receiving the license, the circumstances should be described in detail, and a certificate should be provided, along with two 2.5-inch half-length photos of the person, and submitted to the Education Department through the municipal and county education administrative authorities for verification and reissue. A fee of two yuan must be paid for reissuing the license. Article 14: If, after receiving the license, any of the circumstances listed in Article 5 of these regulations, or any of the circumstances listed in Article 91 of the Elementary School Regulations, or other improper behavior that tarnishes the teaching profession, is found to be true by the Education Department, the license may be revoked. Article 15: Those who possess one of the qualifications listed in Articles 3 and 4 of these regulations must not serve as elementary school teachers unless they have passed the qualification examination and been issued a license. Article 16: The validity period of the qualification certificate will be determined separately. Article 17: Detailed rules for the implementation of the qualification examination will be determined separately. Article 18: These regulations shall be decided by the Hunan Provincial Government Committee and submitted by the Education Department to the Ministry of Education for record and implementation.

▲ Provisional Organizational Regulations of the Elementary School Teacher Qualification Examination Committee of the Education Department of Hunan Province:

Article 1: This committee is established in accordance with the provisions of Article 1 of the Provisional Regulations for the Elementary School Teacher Qualification Examination of the Education Department of Hunan Province to handle all matters related to the qualification examination of elementary school teachers in this province. Article 2: This committee is composed of the following personnel: (1) One Chairman, concurrently held by the Director of the Education Department, who presides over the committee affairs and summarizes the results; (2) One Chief Committee Member, appointed by the Director from among the committee members, who handles the daily affairs of the committee under the command of the Chairman; (3) Nine to eleven Committee Members, appointed or assigned by the Director from among the personnel of the Education Department, who handle all affairs of the committee under the command of the Chairman; (4) A number of Examination Committee Members, appointed by the Director when the examination is implemented, who are in charge of examination affairs under the command of the Chairman. The committee members mentioned in the preceding paragraph, except for the Examination Committee Members, are all unpaid. Article 3: This committee may establish clerical and secretarial positions as appropriate. Article 4: The expenses of this committee shall be determined separately. Article 5: The detailed rules for the operation of this committee shall be determined separately. Article 6: These regulations shall be decided by the Hunan Provincial Government Committee and submitted by the Education Department to the Ministry of Education for record and implementation. (February 16)

Ministry of Education Decides to Establish National Northeast Zhongshan Middle School in North China 241

▲ To Provide Relief to Northeast Youths Deprived of Education

▲ First Establish Seven Classes in Senior and Junior High School

▲ Expected to Open in March This Year

(Nanjing, 20th) In order to provide relief to Northeast youths deprived of education, the Ministry of Education has decided to establish the National Northeast Zhongshan Middle School in North China, with Li Xien, Deputy Director of the Northeast Youths Education Relief Office, concurrently serving as the principal. In this initial phase, three classes each will be established for the first and second semesters of the first year of junior and senior high school, and one class each will be established for junior and senior high school preparatory courses, as well as a junior vocational class, totaling seven classes. It is planned to enroll 600 to 700 students, with classes expected to begin in March. After sufficient equipment has been procured, a senior vocational class will be established after the summer vacation. The current budget is estimated at 8,000 yuan per month, and the school is currently in contact for renting dormitories and school buildings.

Mongolian Prince Interested in Rural Education 242

▲ Guided by Personnel Dispatched by the Ministry of Education

▲ Also Visited Qixia Mountain Rural Normal School

Dispute Arises at Anglo-American Workers' Children School in Shanghai, Delaying the Start of School 248

The Factory Refuses to Provide Funds, and School Has Not Yet Opened

The Municipal Education Bureau Dispatches Personnel to the School for Investigation

The Anglo-American Tobacco Factory Workers' Children School in Pudong was founded by the Cigarette Industry Union of the Former Fifth District. Although the school has repeatedly requested the release of funds, the factory has deliberately created difficulties and turned a deaf ear, leaving the children out of school. Now, in order to protect labor education, Chen Peide and other labor representatives on the board of directors have submitted a report to the Education and Social Bureaus requesting relief. The Municipal Government and the Education Bureau have dispatched Section Chief Feng and Tang Jingxiu to the school for investigation, and have advised the factory to fulfill the resolution of the board of directors and release funds as soon as possible so that the school can open.

According to the person in charge of the school, since Principal Xu took office, he has always prioritized the school and led by example, and there has been no misconduct. Free Talk

How Are Chinese Students? 254

— Fan Zhongyun

Regarding the national characteristics of various European countries, there is a famous story:

"A teacher in a school once gave his students of various nationalities a topic for their exams, and that topic was about elephants. The English student wrote a 'Record of Hunting Elephants in Africa'; the French student wrote a short poem, 'Elephant Love'; the German student wrote a 300-page essay on the subject of elephants, called 'Introduction to the Philosophy of Elephants'; and a Polish student wrote a political essay called 'The Elephant and the Polish Question'."

I saw this story in Yusuke Tsurumi's travelogue of Europe and America, and I couldn't help but wonder what a Chinese student would write if there were one in that school.

I think if it were thirty years ago, then this Chinese student would definitely write an eight-legged essay about elephants, but now it is the era of the Republic of China, and eight-legged essays have long been abolished. Even the ancient prose of Han Yu, Liu Zongyuan, Ouyang Xiu, Su Shi, and even the Tongcheng and Yanghu schools, although some people advocate restoring it, has already died. At this time, what exactly would our Chinese students write?

Then it is still an eight-legged essay, but in vernacular, a new style.

Because the education of writing naturally focuses on the carving of words and sentences, the decoration of essays, a kind of empty and contentless game of writing, and this is precisely the characteristic of Chinese eight-legged essays.

Now, of course, the eight-legged essay has been abolished, and classical Chinese has also been changed to vernacular, but the spirit of the old era is still deeply rooted. School education emphasizes writing, school grades are based on the quality of writing, and national examinations use essays as a standard for selection.

"The emperor values heroes, and writing is what he teaches you. All other professions are inferior, only studying is high," this saying is still very applicable today.

"The Traveler" and "Daughter of the Streets" 255

— Mu Mutian

In the February issue of "Modern," there are two poems that I find noteworthy. One is "The Traveler" (anonymous), and the other is "Daughter of the Streets" (Su Su).

In recent years, good poetry has rarely appeared. Especially in lyrical poems, "romantic" works occupy the majority. Works reflecting society and modernity seem to be in the minority.

It is true that poetry must have a realm. But that realm must be a reflection of society.

In "The Traveler" and "Daughter of the Streets," there are, of course, no large harbors, noisy factories, deep underground mines, jazz-filled dance halls, skyscraper department stores, vast racetracks, and other modern scenes, but they also have profound modernity.

Those two poems deeply express the sorrow of a certain group of people. Naturally, that sorrow is a product of the global economic panic and the collapse of the Chinese countryside.

In "The Traveler," the depression and sorrow of a section of modern petty bourgeoisie are revealed. The poet imagines the "traveler treading wearily on a long journey," "carrying a basket of sorrow," watching their "hesitation" and "hesitation." Isn't this "hesitation" and "hesitation" one of the symbols of the times? For this kind of traveler, the poet instructs: "May you leave from now on, accompanying the exile of Siberia, and sing loudly." What deep sorrow is contained in this emotion of calling people to be wanderers! I think this kind of non-decadent grief is precious. The poet is forever attached to the "happy land" he "loves"! The theme of "The Traveler" has been adopted by many people, but it has never been deepened to this extent. Of course, the use of old rhetoric in this poem is a shortcoming. However, in terms of rhythm, there is no affectation. This also reflects the strong feudal nature in Shanghai.

Su Su's "Daughter of the Streets" is a reflection of the modern economic panic. The material is very realistic. The impoverishment of China has spread to streetwalkers. In this poem, the temporality and spatiality of the subject matter are clearly expressed. We read it again and again, and we don't see any fictional elements at all. Compared with this poem, "The Traveler" is naturally much more empty. The poet vividly expresses that the tragedy happened on the streets of Shanghai recently. The poet uses the two lines "What is annoying is the rainy season of the yellow plum season, she likes the dusk floating up in the moon" to indicate the local background on the one hand, and to express that even the prostitute has to endure the nature's anger. The prostitute "with a cigarette in the corner of her mouth and an empty wallet, walking alone on the cement road," selling coquettishness, winking, waiting for men who buy laughter, but in the end, she has to "walk home anxiously with his empty wallet." That scene is really bleak! But why are there no men buying laughter? That's what she doesn't know. She asks, "Why is this business still declining?" But she can't find a reason. However, "people are turning over like waves in the streets"! The poet links the end of the year with unemployment, and at the same time indicates that she is not the only one who is unemployed. It is "the year red lanterns are piece by piece, and her companions are groups and groups." Are they similarly unemployed? The poet not only describes that lonely prostitute, but also describes the appearance of Shanghai streets at the end of the year, and her group, and also pays attention to the ridicule of the vendors and her habit of that kind of teasing. How realistic is this! This poem has its universality, and it has its individuality. There are no embellished words in the language, and no contrived traces in the rhythm. It is a true poem. I think Su Su is indeed a new poet with a promising future. If we compare this poem with Zang Kejia's "Goddess," we can better understand the value of this poem. Zang Kejia reveals his philosophy of Stoicism through "Goddess," while Su Su is a realistic and faithful describer. I hope that more poems like "Daughter of the Streets" will be produced in the future. Who says that ordinary realistic materials cannot be written in poetry?

Feast 256

— Zhou Lengjia

The banquet begins. The host is the director of a certain department, and the distinguished guest is the newly appointed section chief with the same status. The other seven or eight guests are all unimportant characters, subordinate to the section chief and dependent on the section chief for food and clothing.

This forms a scene that is not commonly seen at ordinary banquets. The host and guest sitting face to face, the director and the section chief, became the big dipper in the sky. The seven or eight section members who were doing the escorting surrounded them on both sides like stars arching the North Star. They seemed to know that they were in a position to help, without freedom of will, nor the right to speak casually, so they were all well-behaved and silent. Apart from saying "Please, please" when a dish was served, they all looked to the director and the section chief. Whenever the director or section chief said a word, some of the section members nodded, and some circled their heads in the air, indicating that this was an undeniable truth that everyone should believe. The more vigorously the director and the section chief spoke, the more vigorously the section members nodded and circled.

At this time, the cook just sent up a pot of stir-fried dishes. The section chief tasted it and seemed to think it tasted very good, and couldn't help but praise:

"This dish tastes good!"

The section members had all clamped a chopstick of dishes and were about to send them to their mouths. Hearing this sentence, they hurriedly nodded and circled. Several people were careless, and their noses touched the dishes, which were painfully hot, but they still echoed and praised in unison:

"It is indeed delicious and extraordinary!"

"I haven't eaten such a delicious dish for many years!"

The host was very happy because the dish was praised. The guest was also very happy because he actually had the opportunity to speak, and this sentence, needless to say, was also like the words of the director or the section chief, which could be included in one of the undeniable truths and had immortal value.

However, unfortunately! The section chief suddenly farted when everyone was silent. The sound was very loud and could not be concealed. Even the section chief himself could not help but feel a little embarrassed. The section members were not convenient to nod or circle, and what was even more hateful was that no one could help but laugh, which made everyone very embarrassed. Fortunately, one of the section members was more clever. He lowered his head and happened to see a dog drilling around under the table, so he kicked it hard. The dog was in pain and yelled "Woof" and ran out with a bone in its mouth. The director said like he was triggered: "There are many stray dogs in the city recently."

Of course, the section members all knew how to help, so they moved the topic to dogs one sentence at a time. Some said that a shelter should be set up for dogs. Some said that it would be better to execute them quickly, tying stones to the dogs and sinking them into the river. Some said that sinking in the river was not good, as it would easily cause an epidemic, so it would be better to use electrocution. After talking about it, even the section chief was very happy to abandon his previous shyness and joined in the conversation. And this fart became an unsolved case, and no one investigated who farted.

After the banquet was over, the guests were sitting and drinking tea. The host director took out a dish of golden silk jujubes from inside and said with exaggerated pride:

"This is a real golden silk jujube from Hong Kong, everyone is welcome, please feel free to use it."

Although it was said that it was free to use, the person who started first still had to let the section chief. He picked up a jujube, put it in his mouth and chewed it. It happened that this jujube had no pit, so he praised it incessantly:

"It's really worthy of being a golden silk jujube from Hong Kong! I think it must have been made using scientific methods, so there is no pit."

This made the section members a little embarrassed, because they had each eaten a jujube, but each jujube had a pit in it. Now hearing the section chief say this, they felt that the section chief's words were justified. Since the section chief said there was no pit, but they spit out the pit, weren't they deliberately opposing the section chief and ruining the section chief's platform? If the section chief was angry and ordered their dismissal, not only would their jobs be broken, but even their families would have to cry for hunger and cold. Thinking like this, they felt that this jujube pit was really a matter of great importance. Therefore, they had to frown and reluctantly swallow this small jujube pit that was as sharp as a steel needle at both ends.

The section chief picked up another jujube and put it in his mouth, but this time he found a pit in the jujube. He couldn't help but exclaim in surprise:

"Why is there a pit in this jujube?"

The director did not pay attention to what the section chief said before, so he said seriously at this time: "Of course jujubes have pits." The section chief still didn't quite believe it, so he asked the section members: "Did you eat a pit?"

The section members were even more embarrassed, they couldn't say that they ate it, nor could they say that they didn't eat it. After a long while, they all said hesitantly: "We ate it."

"We ate it, how come I didn't see you spitting out the pit?" Seeming very annoyed by this answer, the section chief's tone became very serious.

Like a thunderbolt on their heads, the section members couldn't help but look at each other in dismay, feeling that this time their jobs must not be saved. One of the section members became anxious, his throat itched, he coughed dryly, and he actually coughed out the pit. He was very happy and hurriedly took the pit out of his mouth and said: "As expected, it is a golden silk jujube from Hong Kong, even the pit is different from ordinary jujubes."

The other section members were even more panicked when they saw that one of the section members had coughed out the pit, so they all coughed dryly, trying to cough the pit back into their mouths.

The host director was very strange and couldn't help asking: "Why are you all coughing today?"

The section members who had not coughed out the pits were all unable to laugh or cry, and barely smiled and said: "Probably because we drank too much wine today."

Interesting Metaphors 257

— Shu

(X) (Three)

Xiao Shiwei discussed concubines with Mr. Qian, and said to himself, "The scenery in the south is very different from the past, and my mood is increasingly desolate. I rashly want to buy a concubine to provide a little writing," which shows that the "concubine" is a kind of tool to "provide a little writing" when the spirit feels desolate. However, Mr. Xiao was too unlucky, and the result of buying a concubine did not get any comfort. Therefore, he continued to write, "However, it is difficult to get people in a hurry, so it is inevitable to be perfunctory and have only burdens. Is it possible to get a good taste?" It is even more evident that buying a concubine is also a "responsibility" of life, and it takes a lot of effort, otherwise, "perfunctory and negligent" will only "have burdens." Buying a concubine to satisfy one's appetite, at this time, it is naturally impossible to talk about "good taste." This "writing," this "luck," this "negligence," this "good taste," can be said to be the "divine product" in interesting metaphors, not only letting us see the "concubine-marrying view" of the predecessors. Also, whether or not marrying a concubine is satisfactory depends not only on "not being willing to be negligent," but also on the results of previous lives' cultivation. Xiao Shiwei married a concubine and "failed to achieve his ambitions," so he turned to envy others. So he wrote, "I heard that Mr. Weng recently got a beautiful woman, so he is a talented person. It is because of diligent cultivation in past lives that he can obtain this beauty, so I blame myself even more for not working hard enough in my previous life." Are there people who want to marry a concubine in the next life? Why not work hard in this life?

I Curse That Smile of Yours (7) 258

Although it was still an inflexible accent, it turned into an urgent pleading tone. It was as if an honest and lovely child was asking an adult for candy, showing a joyful look, saying:

"I丨丨I want a piece of candy丨丨delicious candy."

The door and walls of the traveler's house are the doors and walls of all the families in the valley, all made of bitter bamboo pieces. Old Woman

Hefeisagirl

New Standard for Margin Gold in the April Period Debuts 259

丨Public Sentiment is Strong and the Market Rises Suddenly丨

Heng Seng Listing Reduced on Both British and American Markets, March Period Also Rose 7.6 Yuan

Total Number of New Chips in the April Period is 6,762

The gold market yesterday saw the new standard for the April period on the market, the situation suddenly developed, public sentiment was also strong, and gold prices rose sharply. Heng Seng listings were reduced by .25 on both British and American markets, so the March period also rose sharply. Early this morning, the overseas silver market saw a consistent rise in the British and American markets, with the forward silver price on the Hong Kong Gold & Silver Exchange rising more than falling, but large trading houses were better. Foreign exchange continued to rise, London spot gold fell 4 pence, US cotton fell 19 pounds, and US wheat fell .875. The opening price of raw materials was 932 yuan, and Shun Mao Yuan, Mao Yong and others took advantage of the low price to take positions, rising to 37-38 yuan, and public sentiment was greatly stimulated. Afterwards, although Sheng Da Heng Tai sold off, retreating to 35-36 yuan, the market conditions were stable. After the opening, banks actively bought, and large investors bought one after another, rising to over 40 yuan. Foreign telegrams reported that US silver production was excessive or that there might be a sell-off, although there was no practical substance, and Sassoon bought British, Guangbang bought American, and Qiao Zhifu also had a settlement. The domestic market was extremely tight, and the Heng Seng listings of British and American exchange rates suddenly shrank, greatly boosting public sentiment, and gold prices soared even higher. Although there were sales at high prices later, it was difficult to retreat into 40 yuan, because Guangbang suddenly came to fiercely replenish, and the morning market was supported, and the afternoon close was also stable. In the afternoon market, foreign telegrams reported that China and the US signed a silver agreement to limit silver sales. The market was afraid of fatigue and fell once, but in the end, the situation stabilized and fluctuated. The raw gold price ranged from 950 yuan to 955 yuan, which has been changed to the market average. Here's a record of the day's market conditions.

The opening price for the April market was 936 yuan, the spot price opened at 6.1 yuan, the foreign exchange market opened with recent selling prices of 1 shilling 4 pence .625 for British exchange and 35.5 yuan for US exchange, then 5.5 yuan. Heng Yu, Yuan Mao Yong, Da De Cheng, Tian Feng, Yong Hong Li Yuan Chun and others jointly entered positions. Detailed Rules for Collecting Special Margin Deposits for Yarn and Cotton Transactions 265

Yesterday, the Yarn Exchange Brokers Association announced a notice regarding the collection of special margin deposits. It stated that it had received a letter from the Exchange stating that the fifth board of directors, at its first meeting, resolved that, effective immediately, the buying and selling quantities and new purchases and sales in the total open accounts of cotton yarn and cotton by all brokers would be subject to the collection of special margin deposits according to the following regulations. The agreed-upon collection methods are listed item by item below:

(1) For each broker's open cotton yarn transactions, from 10,050 bales to 20,000 bales, in addition to the basic margin deposit of 8 yuan (substitutes), a special margin deposit of 4 yuan in cash will be collected per bale.

(2) For each broker's open cotton yarn transactions, from 20,050 bales to 30,000 bales, in addition to the basic margin deposit of 8 yuan (substitutes), a special margin deposit of 8 yuan in cash will be collected per bale.

(3) For each broker's open cotton yarn transactions exceeding 30,000 bales, in addition to the basic margin deposit of 8 yuan (substitutes), a special margin deposit of 16 yuan in cash will be collected per bale.

(4) For each broker's cotton yarn "two-legged" accounts, the special margin deposit will be collected from one side according to the above rates.

(5) For each broker's open cotton transactions, from 20,100 piculs to 40,000 piculs, in addition to the basic margin deposit of 3 yuan (substitutes), a special margin deposit of 2 yuan in cash will be collected per picul.

(6) For each broker's open cotton transactions, from 40,100 piculs to 60,000 piculs, in addition to the basic margin deposit of 3 yuan (substitutes), a special margin deposit of 4 yuan in cash will be collected per picul.

(7) For each broker's open cotton transactions exceeding 60,000 piculs, in addition to the basic margin deposit of 3 yuan (substitutes), a special margin deposit of 6 yuan in cash will be collected per picul.

(8) For each broker's cotton "two-legged" accounts, the special margin deposit will be collected from one side according to the above rates.

(9) No special margin deposit will be collected for each broker's open cotton yarn transactions of less than 10,050 bales or open cotton transactions of less than 20,100 piculs.

(10) For each broker's cotton yarn and cotton transactions, whether for open account quantities or new purchases and sales, all special margin deposits must be paid to the Exchange from today onwards according to the above rates, without delay.

(11) In addition to the above-mentioned rates, the Exchange may increase the special margin deposit at any time as necessary in accordance with the provisions of Article 70 of the Operating Rules.

Fish Market 278

Japanese Fishing Vessels Dump Imports

Fish Market Plunges Yesterday Morning

In recent days, fish prices have been relatively high due to the approaching Lunar New Year (although much lower than at the same time last year). However, yesterday morning, the market plunged due to congested deliveries from various places, such as over 1,000 piculs of Ningbo fresh large and small yellow croaker and butterfly fish. In particular, the Japanese fishing vessel "Wanyi Maru" imported and dumped over 160 piculs of small yellow croaker, sea eel, etc. at reduced prices, leading to a significant drop in fish prices. For example, small yellow croaker was priced at 31 yuan per picul in the previous morning but opened at 26 yuan per picul yesterday morning. However, the final selling price was 15 yuan per picul. Other fish also experienced price declines. Therefore, the lack of a unified plan and distribution for the fish market is insufficient to stabilize it.

Page 17

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Idle Talk

Re-discussing the Rent Reduction Movement 301

— Qiong

In this "Great Shanghai," the first metropolis of the Orient, which is already deeply aware of the economic downturn, the withered market, and even laments its "decline," the land and real estate investment business is a unique and prosperous undertaking. While various businesses here are using methods such as deep discounts, buy-one-get-one-free offers, and even prize draws to attract customers to "graciously come," the sharp rise in land prices and rents cannot be compared with anything. This peculiar fact allows us to see, through the dismal scene of a large number of factory closures and store shutdowns, the construction of many large buildings, mansions, and hotels, and the construction and renovation of countless alleyways and villages. It is these towering and magnificent new buildings that have embellished and decorated a "prosperous Shanghai" during the economic crisis.

This "prosperity," which is outwardly strong but inwardly weak, symbolizes the deepening bankruptcy of China's rural areas, the increasing natural and man-made disasters, and the ancient country, the tail end of international capitalist powers' commodity sales and investments, is becoming increasingly colonialized. The former has resulted in many "nouveau riches" who have made a fortune and are carrying hundreds of thousands around their waists, and "local tycoons" who own thousands of acres of fertile land, bringing "Brother Copper Coin" to Shanghai as a safe haven to live as "gentlemen in retirement." Countless bankrupt farmers also come to this city with their bare hands to sell their labor; while the latter's influence has led to the decline of Chinese industry and commerce. Constant civil wars, natural disasters, and banditry have increased Shanghai's population, raising the demand for housing. The direct impact of foreign goods dumping and the decline of Chinese industry and commerce is driving capital, originally intended for production, to compete to buy land and purchase real estate. This is the source of the sharp rise in land prices and rents in Shanghai. Therefore, in the "prosperity" of Shanghai, we can see a special phenomenon that is both laughable and lamentable. The more bankrupt the Chinese countryside is, the more depressed industry and commerce are, the higher Shanghai's land prices rise and the higher the rents become. The bankruptcy of the countryside and the decline of industry and commerce have become the "heart's desire" of Shanghai's landlords and land tycoons, "the people's suffering." Therefore, many "distinguished people" are also competing to purchase real estate in Shanghai, maintaining Shanghai's "prosperity" and striving for the construction of "Greater Shanghai." One cause, one effect, can be said to have greatly attained the way of governance and chaos.

However, under this "prosperity," the millions of Shanghai citizens who live by selling their labor and renting houses are groaning, tossing and turning, struggling helplessly. This sound of miserable cries and wails, like mosquitoes gathering into thunder, has given rise to the recent rent reduction movement. When we think of the ugly faces of the big landlords and sub-landlords at the beginning and end of the month when they demand rent, pressing and urging payment, and the viciousness of carrying out evictions and then going to the police, it is indeed as the slogan of the Rent Reduction Movement Committee says: "Reducing rent to relieve the people's distress" is indeed a fact that "three million Shanghai citizens yearn for." And the letter from various organizations in the city to the Water and Wood Industry Union: "Blood and sweat are insufficient, resorting to pawn and sale, pawn and sale are exhausted, only to risk life." That "even if not imprisoned, one will surely turn to the gutter" directly points out the suffering of the three million citizens of Shanghai. At a time when the tide of economic crisis is sweeping the entire world, reducing rent, although not able to "revive the market and prosper Shanghai," is indeed a brave and meaningful resistance of impoverished citizens in despair against the "asset-boasting" big landlords. Because we can say that for the general citizens and laborers of Shanghai, in the torment of "making a living with difficulty," in the struggle of poverty and unemployment, the annually increasing rent is the heaviest oppression to bear, and perhaps one of the major causes of various crimes such as murder and suicide.

The Antagonistic Nature of Life 302

— Nai Shuo

This, of course, can be said; if there are good aspects to human nature, then I think understanding and compassion are the best parts of that good.

If one can understand, then estrangement will not occur; and animosity will not arise between people. If, in addition to understanding, one can also sympathize, then not only will animosity not arise, but these people will be easier to win over. From there, the so-called mutual assistance in the world, as well as various good deeds of self-sacrifice, will appear in the interaction between these people.

Therefore, generally, whether elderly or young, knowledgeable people always believe that the inability of mankind to fully exert these good deeds of mankind is undeniably the greatest regret among us humans. This is especially deeply felt by those who have bad wives, or who have concubines in addition to their wives.

Originally, according to the philosophy of hedonism, life is nothing more than seeking stimulation. According to the interpretation of this school of thought, it means that one should never waste life, but enjoy every moment. Because having more enjoyment is always more fulfilling than not having it. And if one dies soon, it will be easier to close one's eyes. Thus, those who are tired of their wives, or who have become tired of them and taken concubines, always feel that "understanding" and "compassion" must be vigorously helped to develop, unafraid that "understanding" and "compassion" already permeate all the minute things in life.

Those who think this way do so because their wives do not allow them to associate with other women besides themselves, or to marry concubines. Therefore, their fierce resistance and fierce scolding are naturally the highest expressions of not understanding and not sympathizing. And if one can know their philosophy and not be surprised by their deep feelings, then naturally one will not be surprised.

But isn't that naturally so? Men earn money, and women sit and eat. So the reason why women are born beautiful is to be played with by men. But this fun and beauty only lasts for a few short years and months. After these years, of course, they are even more annoying than worn-out shoes. Therefore, while keeping her alive and providing her with some money and goods to maintain her life, one secretly or openly goes outside to find another woman to play with. Or, one takes the woman one plays with as a concubine, which is thought to be the most humane and fairest thing to do. Why can't you always be beautiful, and why don't you go and earn money?

However, wives are always incomprehensible, and without understanding, there is no sympathy. And since the best part of this human nature is so suppressed, destroyed, vilified, and hindered from developing by them, naturally these knowledgeable gentlemen think it is a great regret.

Her Understanding 303

— Shu Xian

When she was very young, she worked in a factory. At that time, she was young and had little knowledge, and she couldn't see whether this huge society was "white," "red," or "black."

It seemed that these conversations aroused her great interest, although many of them she did not fully understand due to her age, but they were all mysterious riddles that were deeply worth her thinking and guessing.

Her physical condition slowly began to change strangely, such as the pain of the whole body's muscles and bones, and the bulging breasts as if they were tightly bound by cloth, making her feel very painful.

The environment constantly gave her many irregular stimuli, and she began to flirt with the male workers. Whenever the male worker's hand touched her face or pinched her leg, the blood in her whole body would boil, and her nerves would immediately feel a special, indescribable comfort. Now she already had a "sexual" desire, yearning for "fleshly" comfort!

Loss of Happiness 304

Mr. Editor:

Through a friend's introduction, I engaged a Miss Zhu as my wife, and we have been married for several years. However, our relationship is not harmonious, leading to the loss of my happiness. I am a businessman who is often away on business. Currently, there is a third party who wishes to enter into a lifelong agreement with me. I understand this third party is already betrothed to a Mr. Zhang. Would marrying me be prohibited by law? As a merchant, I cannot afford the expenses of two households. I want to discuss a divorce with my current wife privately, without going through legal procedures, and create a divorce agreement, each keeping a copy. Afterward, I would marry the third party. I am unsure if this is legally permissible. Therefore, I take the liberty of writing to you, humbly requesting that you trouble yourself to provide a clear explanation in the newspaper. I respectfully wish you

Peace and Health,

Li Xiong森 sincerely submits

Editor's Note: Mr. Li's inquiry has two main points: First, can a woman who is already engaged to someone else become engaged to another person? Second, can a divorce be conducted without legal procedures, through mutual agreement? The second point is not much of a problem, as the law originally stipulated "voluntary divorce." (See "Why Does Divorce Become Difficult?" in this mailbox on February 10th.) However, voluntary divorce requires mutual consent as a prerequisite. This is what Mr. Li should pay attention to. In addition, voluntary divorce should be in writing and have the signatures of at least two witnesses. The first question is more complex because a woman who is already engaged should not become engaged to another person before the original engagement is dissolved. However, an engagement is a type of contract, and its effect is not very strong. Even if one party breaches the contract, the other party can only request compensation for damages and cannot request the court to enforce the contract. Therefore, the "third party" is not absolutely forbidden from marrying Mr. Li, but it is best to have the "third party" dissolve the original engagement with Mr. Zhang first. (There has been frequent discussion about dissolving engagements in this mailbox recently. Mr. Li and readers can refer back to those discussions. No need to repeat them here.)

Novel

Husband and Wife (4) 305

— Yu Mei

With eyes that saw the relationship between men and women as an old man would, Xu San watched him smoke. A tiny, short iron skewer held a seed-like particle, which he turned over the flame, sometimes swelling, sometimes emitting a wisp of steam. Then, holding it on his left forefinger, he did this ten times, until the black particle stuck to the hole in the pipe. He pulled out the needle, burned the black particle over the flame to press it down, and then heated the smoke skewer. He poked a small hole in the pipe. At that moment, Manager Zhao seemed to remember something and suddenly leaned forward, saying to Su Ba, who was sitting on the floor mat next to Xu San,

"Lao Ba, have a hit. It's ready, freshly made."

"I wouldn't dare. No, thank you, Mr. Zhao. I've already eaten."

"Come on, the same, freshly made." Manager Zhao sat back down after leaning forward.

"Really, no, Mr. Zhao, please invite Mr. Cao."

Mr. Cao, after declining for a long time, took the pipe and said to Xu San, "Lao San, you..."

"No, Mr. Cao, please have it," Xu San quickly declined.

So, as Mr. Cao's lips touched the pipe, Manager Zhao's head fell back onto the pillow. The whole room was filled with lively sounds. On this small bed that was a world apart, only the sound of the paste being sucked into the pipe could be heard.

Because his right hand was on top, Manager Zhao smoked the second pipe.

Inside, at one of the gambling tables, there was a sudden moment of tension, followed by a loud noise, a "board" had passed. Soon, the tense atmosphere relaxed again, with only the sound of money. Everyone settled their accounts, and then someone loudly called out,

"I'm pushing a board. Fifty yuan, who's a shareholder?"

"I'm a shareholder." Someone quickly replied.

"Okay, wah, come on!" Many other voices joined in.

Everyone relaxed a little, some changed direction, and immediately gathered together again. Two people walked over to the tobacco area. One lay down, squeezing his tired body among the people lying haphazardly on the floor mat. One person was awakened by the newcomer, asking hazily and somewhat alarmed,

"What's wrong? What's wrong?"

"San Heshang and Wu Dachui pushed again."

"Okay, let's go!" The person who had just woken up suddenly sat up, felt for his shoes by the edge of the floor mat, and said, "Su Ba, how are you doing? Let's hit it once."

"Let's see how the wind blows, okay."

Su Ba went with him. The other newcomer who had left the scene sat down behind Xu San, in Su Ba's place, and Chang Fa also left.

Xu San, who also wanted to try his luck, remained seated on the floor mat, watching the opium lamp. He was contemplating many things in his heart. He wanted to bet on the red side five times in a row, thus winning ten yuan, and then go home and give five yuan to his wife, who would be so happy that she wouldn't even want to get out of bed the next morning. However, the money placed on the dealer might be lost all at once, so it would be safer and more reliable to share a little bit of the initial stake. His life was sustained in the lamplight and the sounds of the gambling.

Manager Zhao left. Zhou Chunrong, who had won the previous "board," came over. Zhou Chunrong's face was flushed, and his heart was filled with the joy of victory. He took out a yuan and handed it to Xu San, saying,

"Go home and get a yuan's worth of tobacco."

Movie Special Issue

George Raft's Awe of Women (Part 1) 306

— Mi Qi

As everyone knows, George Raft is a movie star who is most popular with women on the screen. Many people say his appearance is similar to the late

Rudolph Valentino), which is why he is even more worshipped by women. When he lived in New York and worked on the stage, his theater was packed with women every day, surrounding him so much that he had to sneak in and out through the back door. But he is a star who is most afraid of women. A Hollywood reporter recently had a conversation with him. He didn't avoid the topic and openly stated many of his opinions about women and the reasons why he is in awe of women and dare not approach them. Here are some of them.

He said, "I have been afraid of women since I was a child. This is not just me, many Hollywood stars are like this because there are too many women with a wild nature who always want to take advantage and extort money." These were his bold words. Some people say he shouldn't publicly say such things and insult women because how he got his star status… wasn't it mostly because women were obsessed with his looks and acting and desperately supported him? George Raft is still not married. But he doesn't live alone either, because he doesn't dare to live alone. He always has a male companion living with him. When he goes out, he always has a male companion following him like a bodyguard. In Hollywood, few people see him go out with a woman. The only one is Marjorie King. Why isn't he afraid of Marjorie? Because he is prepared to marry her. Although their wedding date hasn't been announced yet, they will eventually become husband and wife sooner or later.

George Raft has had too many and too surprising experiences with women in his life, which have exhausted his natural feelings for women. He said, "Now, lawsuits for breach of promise or abandonment are so popular in Hollywood that they are almost like kidnappings. No matter what star, he is likely to be framed anytime, anywhere. Not long ago, I gave a woman two thousand dollars. Actually, I can't even remember where I met her. At that time, I had just finished filming a movie and still had entanglements with the company, so although I knew that if I went to court with that woman, I would definitely win, I didn't want to fight a lawsuit with her. First, I was afraid of the publicity in the newspapers, which would damage my reputation, so I settled with her privately. But if I wasn't a movie star, I would have been unforgiving to her. But then again, if I wasn't a movie star, that woman wouldn't have had the idea of extorting money from me. They really see movie stars as 'good accounts' that are easy to be intimidated and extorted."

"That woman had another reason for wanting to extort money. She came to Hollywood and couldn't find a way to show her fame. She wanted her name to be published in large letters in the newspapers with mine so that she could become famous in one fell swoop. But I was smarter than her. I never told the reporters her name, and she was also afraid to announce it herself, fearing that a lawsuit would really be filed. Therefore, her plan failed except for getting a little money." (To be continued)

Film Review

Review of "Footlight Parade" 307

— Ya Fu

Footlight Parade – Cathay

Following "42nd Street" and "Gold Diggers of 1933," Warner Brothers has this "Footlight Parade."

Almost every musical film is the same. A story is often secondary, and the story is just a series of songs and dances. Likewise, "Footlight Parade" is the same. Other than the song and dance scenes, it is just a mediocre story. We can almost imagine that love, conflicts between men and women, and even when we see that the female secretary and Kang De are getting along, even though he is in love with Wei Wei, he will definitely marry the female secretary in the end. There is no need to read the instructions in advance.

Here, the playwright is most concerned with emphasizing Kang De's artistic views. Like Wei Ya, stage people finally have to engage in stage art, and unemployed directors eventually become famous through extreme efforts. Isn't that right? When he angrily leaves the company and refuses to cooperate with Gote and others and writes his own name on the advertisement on the street, he suddenly sees a group of black children bathing and immediately sacrifices his prejudices and tries his best to save the failing success.

Indeed, we cannot ignore that Kang De is an unfortunate genius playwright who is unemployed. He gets funding from others to engage in his own business and also helps hundreds of unemployed dancers. If he gives up his position, wouldn't he make those dancers unemployed again? Saving oneself and helping others is the doctrine of the recovery movement. In addition, there is a song and dance scene at the end praising the Blue Eagle Movement, which is enough to prove that the main purpose of this film is to respond to President Roosevelt's recovery movement. Therefore, in addition to some tasteless love stories, we must also understand it in this way.

In terms of the composition of the story, it is not as serious as "42nd Street." However, in terms of the song and dance scenes, it not only surpasses "42nd Street" but is also more gorgeous and grand than "Gold Diggers of 1933." In this aspect alone, it is undoubtedly the unprecedented American musical film. United Artists' "Broadway Bad" or Paramount's "Sitting Pretty" cannot compare

Splendid and gorgeous, the ultimate in luxury and extravagance of American films.

There are four song and dance scenes in total. The first is the cat scene, which is already original and unique. The second is the Grand Hotel, which is more complex than the first. The third is the most exciting scene, with groups of women dancing in the water. Using all the skills of the camera, it shows the most advanced expression of capitalist films' exaggeration. The fourth is a scene praising the Blue Eagle Movement. After a big fight, the human body is arranged into an eagle emblem.

There are two points worth noting about this aspect

(1) The general stage plays on the screen still take into account the fixed position of the stage. Although they use the special skills of photography to make them cinematic, the whole is still restricted by the position of the stage. Such as "42nd Street" or "Gold Diggers of 1933" are all like this. But this highlights the scope of the stage and completely becomes a cinematic song and dance. Except for the first time, the remaining three times are all the time and space of the movie. Especially the third time, from the mountain to the pool, from the water to the fountain, is completely a movie method that cannot be done on the stage.

(2) Generally, musical films put the biggest scene at the end to leave the audience with a relaxed and happy impression. But this is not the case here. Except for the first time that appeared before the story itself, after the story is completely finished, there are three more scenes. And the most lively third scene is not placed at the end. On the contrary, like "Gold Diggers of 1933," it puts the one with meaning at the end, giving people a serious stimulus. "Gold Diggers of 1933" ends with a scene of helping the unemployed, and here it is a praise of the Blue Eagle Movement. In terms of weight, the latter may not be as good as the former, but in any case, neither will give people a very pleasant feeling. It is said that the director of "Gold Diggers of 1933" argued with the company for a long time about the placement of the scene to help the unemployed, and the result was to put it at the end. This is where the artist is unwilling to completely cater to the audience's habits. Of course, "Footlight Parade" is also the same, and it is also worth our attention.

In addition, there is nothing more to say. No matter how well the director Lloyd Bacon grasped the fast melody of the whole tone, and no matter how appropriately he dominated the scenes other than the song and dance, it is still that there is nothing to see except for the song and dance. Naturally, this is an unprecedented great American musical film. It is also a typical capitalist film.

Audience Opinion

Thoughts on Watching "Homecoming" 308

— Ke Xin

When an artistic work is empty or weak in content, no matter how much the author studies in form or technique, it is ultimately difficult to tightly grasp the audience's heart and give a deep impression. The film "Homecoming" is an example. Its material is mediocre and old, and there is not enough authenticity; the intention is not in-depth; the structure is clichéd, making the house fall into a state of poverty and emptiness. However, the director can deal with such a simple story from those small details to make the audience not feel bored, which is quite a success. However, some of the performances of the set design, lighting, and actors are not sufficient, which cannot but be said to be the director's neglect.

The performance on the screen should of course be centered on the actors, and the setting should not only not hinder the actors' actions; performance, but also help the actors' actions and performance, just like the clouds in the painting set off the moon, the clouds not only do not hinder the moon, but also help the moon to be presented more clearly. In this regard, the screen is a bit similar to dance. If we look at the set design of "Homecoming" from this point of view, there are some shortcomings in some places. The most obvious is the living room (?) in the villa, which displays so many antiques, which are arranged there like a big archway, because the space it occupies on the screen is so large, and its fragmentedness diverts the audience's attention, making the audience's vision unable to fully concentrate on the actions of the actors in that scene; this not only does not help the actors, but also hinders them. This shortcoming is not only in "Homecoming," but also often exists in many other Chinese and foreign films.

Regarding lighting, we all know that its function is not only to illuminate things, but also to elicit emotions and create an atmosphere. If we use it well, it is of great help to the performance; otherwise, it will lose its effectiveness and destroy the mood of the play. For example, in "Homecoming," when Jian'er is sick, the light that her mother secretly peeks at outside is still as strong as usual, which is not in harmony with the mood of that scene. If the light is made softer, or even colder, wouldn't the atmosphere that the scene should have been created, completing a harmonious and more moving picture? (To be continued)

Review of "A Movie Star" 309

— Lü Yi

The ending of the Li film is a major flaw. Since Liu Si has become aware of being played with, then she can be allowed to find a bright path. Why should she go to the old residence of her previous husband to suffer a mockery? Is this mockery what Liu Si should suffer? The creation of this unfortunate incident is not Liu Si's fault. If the environment did not force Qiu Shuang to owe debts, and if their family economy was more comfortable, Liu Si would never have fallen to this point.

However, exposing a capitalist who plays with women and a sycophantic class who flatters has been done quite well. Trampling on women is the nature of the bourgeoisie. He has money, and in this society where money can make the devil push the mill, let alone a weak-willed woman. With the leisure class, there is of course also the sycophantic class. Zhou Yunping in this film is an example. However, he wants to flatter, he wants to brag, which is also for money! Therefore, people like He Gongzhe are hateful; people like Zhou Yunping are pitiful.

He Gongzhe's wife's appearance is unnecessary. She is also written too unreasonably. She sees her husband bring a woman to live with him, and she not only does not object, but also uses her like a servant, even a lamb will make a few calls when it is in pain, let alone a person

Now we want to mention Hu Shan's sensual scene, which is the so-called "sacrificing appearance." I really don't understand why the producers don't offer the audience the complete content, but use women's bodies to attract the audience? Or it can be said: this is also for "money"! I am silent, I am speechless.

Queen Christina (10) (1) 310

— Hu Chen

After a pause, Magnus changed the subject and said, "Your Majesty looks radiant today, a beauty never seen before." Christina said, "Magnus, I thank you for all the compliments on my appearance because you are an expert at dealing with women." Magnus said, "Your Majesty's favor is truly grand, but this grand favor has not warmed my heart. What you have given me is just a few crumbs, and the whole has indeed been reserved for others." Christina's pace moved. She said to Magnus impatiently, "Magnus, what exactly are you trying to get to the bottom of?" Suddenly, Magnus hugged her tightly. After a while, she walked away quickly.

That day, a grand banquet was held in the palace to welcome the newly appointed Spanish ambassador. Senior military officers wore full dress uniforms, cabinet ministers wore grand dress, and noble ladies were all dressed up in colorful clothes and jewels. Queen Christina arrived, and the orchestra played intricate music. She sat upright on the throne, with a prototype of the Swedish crown attached above the throne. Her heart was pounding because in just a moment, the young Spanish envoy was about to appear before her. After a while, the master of ceremonies loudly recited the Spanish envoy's full name and official title. The huge palace doors opened, and the orchestra played the Spanish national anthem again. Ambassador Antonio walked quickly into the great hall under the salute of the royal guard, followed by a group of subordinates and attendants dressed in extremely fancy clothes. When he approached the throne, Christina's breathing became short, but she could still imagine how shocked he should be, happy shock. The ambassador walked forward, and in front of him was just a colorful brilliance. The queen sitting at the end of the throne also seemed like a golden sacred being, and he dared not look at her directly, so he walked closer, glanced at her slightly, and knelt down on one knee, with his head bowed to show obedience and respect. Unexpectedly, the queen on the throne opened her mouth. She said, "It is a great honor to welcome your Excellency to our court today."

Antonio felt that the voice was very familiar, and quickly raised his head. Only then did he see that the queen sitting above was the queen he had met on the road the other day. He panicked for a moment, not knowing what to do. He also remembered, just kneeling with his knees bent, looking at her reproachfully. After a while, the queen continued, "Please convey my gratitude to your king, for being able to send someone like you to our country, it is truly a supreme honor." Magnus, the minister of finance standing next to him, looked at the ambassador and the queen, from the queen to the ambassador.
